### USB Devices

Supported Properties by Device

<!--NI_TOPIC bundle=ni-daqmx-labview-api-ref path=menus/categories/measurement/daqmx-mnu.html language=enus -->
## TOPIC 00520: DAQmx - Data Acquisition

- bundle_id: `ni-daqmx-labview-api-ref`
- source_path: `menus/categories/measurement/daqmx-mnu.html`
- source_url: https://docs-be.ni.com/bundle/ni-daqmx-labview-api-ref/raw/resource/enus/menus/categories/measurement/daqmx-mnu.html
- document_id: `ni-daqmx-labview-api-ref`
- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: `reference`
- source_description: Use the NI-DAQmx VIs with your NI-DAQ and NI-Switch hardware devices to develop instrumentation, acquisition, and control applications. icon

### DAQmx - Data Acquisition

Use the NI-DAQmx VIs with your NI-DAQ and NI-Switch hardware devices to develop instrumentation, acquisition, and control applications.

[IMAGE alt='icon' src='daqmx-mnu.png']

- [DAQmx Task Name](../../../constants/daqmx-task-name.html) Lists all tasks you create and save by using the DAQ Assistant . You cannot use this constant to select multiple tasks. Right-click the constant, and select I/O Name Filtering from the shortcut menu to limit the tasks that the constant displays and to limit what you can enter in the constant.
- [DAQmx Global Channel](../../../constants/daqmx-global-channel.html) Lists all virtual channels you create and save using the DAQ Assistant . Select Browse to select multiple channels. Right-click the constant and select I/O Name Filtering from the shortcut menu to limit the channels that the constant displays and to limit what you can enter in the constant.
- [DAQmx Create Virtual Channel VI](../../../vi-lib/daqmx/create/channels-llb/daqmx-create-virtual-channel-vi.html) Creates a virtual channel or set of virtual channels and adds them to a task . The instances of this polymorphic VI correspond to the I/O type of the channel, such as analog input, digital output, or counter output; the measurement or generation to perform, such as temperature measurement, voltage generation, or event counting; and in some cases, the sensor to use, such as a thermocouple or RTD for temperature measurements.
- [DAQmx Read VI](../../../vi-lib/daqmx/read-llb/daqmx-read-vi.html) Reads samples from the task or virtual channels you specify. The instances of this polymorphic VI specify what format of samples to return, whether to read a single sample or multiple samples at once, and whether to read from one or multiple channels.
- [DAQmx Write VI](../../../vi-lib/daqmx/write-llb/daqmx-write-vi.html) Writes samples to the task or virtual channels you specify. The instances of this polymorphic VI specify the format of the samples to write, whether to write one or multiple samples, and whether to write to one or multiple channels.
- [DAQmx Wait Until Done VI](../../../vi-lib/daqmx/configure/task-llb/daqmx-wait-until-done-vi.html) Waits for the measurement or generation to complete. Use this VI to ensure that the specified operation is complete before you stop the task.
- [DAQmx Timing VI](../../../vi-lib/daqmx/configure/timing-llb/daqmx-timing-vi.html) Configures the number of samples to acquire or generate and creates a buffer when needed. The instances of this polymorphic VI correspond to the type of timing to use for the task .
- [DAQmx Trigger VI](../../../vi-lib/daqmx/configure/trigger-llb/daqmx-trigger-vi.html) Configures triggering for the task. The instances of this polymorphic VI correspond to the trigger and trigger type to configure.
- [DAQmx Start Task VI](../../../vi-lib/daqmx/configure/task-llb/daqmx-start-task-vi.html) Transitions the task to the running state to begin the measurement or generation. Using this VI is required for some applications and is optional for others.
- [DAQmx Stop Task VI](../../../vi-lib/daqmx/configure/task-llb/daqmx-stop-task-vi.html) Stops the task and returns it to the state the task was in before the DAQmx Start Task VI ran or the DAQmx Write VI ran with the autostart input set to TRUE.
- [DAQmx Clear Task VI](../../../vi-lib/daqmx/configure/task-llb/daqmx-clear-task-vi.html) Clears the task . Before clearing, this VI aborts the task, if necessary, and releases any resources the task reserved. You cannot use a task after you clear it unless you recreate the task.
- [DAQmx Channel Property Node](../../../vi-lib/daqmx/configure/channels-llb/daqmx-channel-property-node-vi.html) A Property Node with the DAQmx Channel class preselected. Right-click the Property Node and choose Select Filter from the shortcut menu to make the Property Node show only the properties supported by a particular device installed in the system or supported by all devices installed in the system.
- [DAQmx Timing Property Node](../../../vi-lib/daqmx/configure/timing-llb/daqmx-timing-property-node-vi.html) A Property Node with the DAQmx Timing class preselected. Right-click the Property Node and choose Select Filter from the shortcut menu to make the Property Node show only the properties supported by a particular device installed in the system or supported by all the devices installed in the system.
- [DAQmx Trigger Property Node](../../../vi-lib/daqmx/configure/trigger-llb/daqmx-trigger-property-node-vi.html) A Property Node with the DAQmx Trigger class preselected. Right-click the Property Node and choose Select Filter from the shortcut menu to make the Property Node show only the properties supported by a particular device installed in the system or supported by all the devices installed in the system.
- [DAQmx Read Property Node](../../../vi-lib/daqmx/read-llb/daqmx-read-property-node-vi.html) A Property Node with the DAQmx Read class preselected. Right-click the Property Node and choose Select Filter from the shortcut menu to make the Property Node show only the properties supported by a particular device installed in the system or supported by all the devices installed in the system.
- [DAQmx Write Property Node](../../../vi-lib/daqmx/write-llb/daqmx-write-property-node-vi.html) A Property Node with the DAQmx Write class preselected. Right-click the Property Node and choose Select Filter from the shortcut menu to make the Property Node show only the properties supported by a particular device installed in the system or supported by all the devices installed in the system.
- [DAQ Assistant](../../../vi-lib/express/daqmx/daqassistantblock-llb/daqmx-assistant-block-vi.html) Creates, edits, and runs tasks using NI-DAQmx. Refer to the NI-DAQmx Readme for a complete listing of devices NI-DAQmx supports.
- [DAQmx Real-Time](../../../menus/categories/measurement/daqmx/realtime-mnu.html) Use the DAQmx Real Time VIs and function to configure and perform real-time operations.
- [DAQmx Device Configuration](../../../menus/categories/measurement/daqmx/hwspc-mnu.html) Use the DAQmx Device Configuration VIs and functions for hardware-specific configuration and control.
- [DAQmx Advanced Task Options](../../../menus/categories/measurement/daqmx/advtask-mnu.html) Use the Advanced Task Options VIs and functions for advanced configuration and control of tasks.
- [DAQmx Advanced](../../../menus/categories/measurement/daqmx/advprog-mnu.html) Use the Advanced VIs and functions to access advanced and miscellaneous features of NI-DAQmx.

<!--NI_TOPIC bundle=ni-daqmx-labview-api-ref path=menus/categories/measurement/daqmx/advevrtg-mnu.html language=enus -->
## TOPIC 00521: DAQmx Signal Routing

- bundle_id: `ni-daqmx-labview-api-ref`
- source_path: `menus/categories/measurement/daqmx/advevrtg-mnu.html`
- source_url: https://docs-be.ni.com/bundle/ni-daqmx-labview-api-ref/raw/resource/enus/menus/categories/measurement/daqmx/advevrtg-mnu.html
- document_id: `ni-daqmx-labview-api-ref`
- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: `reference`
- source_description: Use the DAQmx Signal Routing VIs for routing signals from one terminal to another. icon

### DAQmx Signal Routing

Use the DAQmx Signal Routing VIs for routing signals from one terminal to another.

[IMAGE alt='icon' src='advevrtg-mnu.png']

- [DAQmx Connect Terminals VI](../../../../vi-lib/daqmx/configure/routing-llb/daqmx-connect-terminals-vi.html) Creates a route between a source and destination terminal . The route can carry a variety of digital signals, such as triggers, clocks, and hardware events.
- [DAQmx Disconnect Terminals VI](../../../../vi-lib/daqmx/configure/routing-llb/daqmx-disconnect-terminals-vi.html) Removes signal routes you created by using the DAQmx Connect Terminals VI. The DAQmx Disconnect Terminals VI cannot remove task-based routes, such as those you create through timing and triggering configuration.
- [DAQmx Tristate Output Terminal VI](../../../../vi-lib/daqmx/configure/routing-llb/daqmx-tristate-output-terminal-vi.html) Sets a terminal to high-impedance state . If you connect an external signal to a terminal on the I/O connector, the terminal must be in high-impedance state. Otherwise, the device could double-drive the terminal and damage the hardware. If you use this VI on a terminal in an active route, the VI fails and returns an error.

Parent topic:

DAQmx Advanced

<!--NI_TOPIC bundle=ni-daqmx-labview-api-ref path=menus/categories/measurement/daqmx/advprog-mnu.html language=enus -->

### DAQmx Advanced

Use the Advanced VIs and functions to access advanced and miscellaneous features of NI-DAQmx.

[IMAGE alt='icon' src='advprog-mnu.png']

- [DAQmx Signal Routing](../../../../menus/categories/measurement/daqmx/advevrtg-mnu.html) Use the DAQmx Signal Routing VIs for routing signals from one terminal to another.
- [DAQmx Calibration](../../../../menus/categories/measurement/daqmx/calib-mnu.html) Use the DAQmx Calibration VIs and functions to perform internal and external calibration of devices.
- [DAQmx System Setup](../../../../menus/categories/measurement/daqmx/syscfg-mnu.html) Use the DAQmx System Setup functions to query information about your devices and software configuration from Measurement & Automation Explorer.
- [DAQmx Scale Setup](../../../../menus/categories/measurement/daqmx/progcreation-mnu.html) Use the DAQmx Scale Setup VIs and property nodes for custom scale creation and configuration.
- [DAQmx Constants & Property Nodes](../../../../menus/categories/measurement/daqmx/ioconstants-mnu.html) The DAQmx Constants and Property Nodes palette contains all I/O constants and property nodes used in NI-DAQmx
- [DAQmx TEDS](../../../../menus/categories/measurement/daqmx/teds-mnu.html) Use the DAQmx TEDS VIs and function to configure physical channels to use and to retrieve TEDS information from a physical channel.
- [DAQmx Utilities](../../../../menus/categories/measurement/daqmx/advutilities-mnu.html) Use the DAQmx Utilities VIs as helper VIs to make NI-DAQmx programming easier.
- [DAQmx Events](../../../../menus/categories/measurement/daqmx/events-mnu.html) Use the DAQmx Events VIs and functions for event-driven programming using NI-DAQmx.

## TOPIC 00523: DAQmx Advanced Task Options

- bundle_id: `ni-daqmx-labview-api-ref`
- source_path: `menus/categories/measurement/daqmx/advtask-mnu.html`
- source_url: https://docs-be.ni.com/bundle/ni-daqmx-labview-api-ref/raw/resource/enus/menus/categories/measurement/daqmx/advtask-mnu.html
- document_id: `ni-daqmx-labview-api-ref`
- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: `reference`
- source_description: Use the Advanced Task Options VIs and functions for advanced configuration and control of tasks. icon

### DAQmx Advanced Task Options

Use the Advanced Task Options VIs and functions for advanced configuration and control of tasks.

[IMAGE alt='icon' src='advtask-mnu.png']

- [DAQmx Create Task VI](../../../../vi-lib/daqmx/create/task-llb/daqmx-create-task-vi.html) Creates a task and adds virtual channels to that task if you specify them in the global virtual channels input. If you specify a task to copy , this VI duplicates the configuration of the specified task in the newly created task before it adds any additional global virtual channels.
- [DAQmx Control Task VI](../../../../vi-lib/daqmx/configure/task-llb/daqmx-control-task-vi.html) Alters the state of a task according to the action you specify.
- [DAQmx Is Task Done VI](../../../../vi-lib/daqmx/configure/task-llb/daqmx-is-task-done-vi.html) Queries the status of the task and indicates if it completed execution. Use this VI to ensure that the specified operation is complete before you stop the task.
- [DAQmx Wait for Valid Timestamp VI](../../../../vi-lib/daqmx/configure/task-llb/daqmx-wait-for-valid-timestamp-vi.html) Wait until the specified timestamp has a value. Use this VI to ensure the timestamp has a valid value to prevent an error when querying a timestamp value.
- [DAQmx Configure Input Buffer VI](../../../../vi-lib/daqmx/configure/buffer-llb/daqmx-configure-input-buffer-vi.html) Overrides the automatic input buffer allocation that NI-DAQmx performs.
- [DAQmx Configure Output Buffer VI](../../../../vi-lib/daqmx/configure/buffer-llb/daqmx-configure-output-buffer-vi.html) Overrides the automatic output buffer allocation that NI-DAQmx performs.
- [DAQmx Configure Logging VI](../../../../vi-lib/daqmx/configure/task-llb/daqmx-configure-logging-vi.html) Configures TDMS file logging for the task.
- [DAQmx Start New File VI](../../../../vi-lib/daqmx/configure/task-llb/daqmx-start-new-file-vi.html) Starts a new TDMS file the next time data is written to disk.
- [DAQmx Task Property Node](../../../../vi-lib/daqmx/configure/task-llb/daqmx-task-property-node-vi.html) A Property Node with the DAQmx Task class preselected. Right-click the Property Node and choose Select Filter from the shortcut menu to make the Property Node show only the properties supported by a particular device installed in the system or supported by all the devices installed in the system.
- [DAQmx Buffer Property Node](../../../../vi-lib/daqmx/configure/buffer-llb/daqmx-buffer-property-node-vi.html) A Property Node with the DAQmx Buffer class preselected. Right-click the Property Node and choose Select Filter from the shortcut menu to make the Property Node show only the properties supported by a particular device installed in the system or supported by all the devices installed in the system.
- [DAQmx Export Signal](../../../../menus/categories/measurement/daqmx/eventrtg-mnu.html) Use the DAQmx Export Signal VI and functions to configure and route control signals within a device or from one device to another.

Parent topic:

DAQmx - Data Acquisition

## TOPIC 00524: DAQmx Utilities

- bundle_id: `ni-daqmx-labview-api-ref`
- source_path: `menus/categories/measurement/daqmx/advutilities-mnu.html`
- source_url: https://docs-be.ni.com/bundle/ni-daqmx-labview-api-ref/raw/resource/enus/menus/categories/measurement/daqmx/advutilities-mnu.html
- document_id: `ni-daqmx-labview-api-ref`
- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: `reference`
- source_description: Use the DAQmx Utilities VIs as helper VIs to make NI-DAQmx programming easier. icon

### DAQmx Utilities

Use the DAQmx Utilities VIs as helper VIs to make NI-DAQmx programming easier.

[IMAGE alt='icon' src='advutilities-mnu.png']

- [DAQmx Flatten Channel String VI](../../../../vi-lib/daqmx/miscellaneous-llb/daqmx-flatten-channel-string-vi.html) Converts an array of physical or virtual channel names to a comma-delimited list of names. You can use this VI to convert an array of channel names to a single string prior to using the DAQmx Create Virtual Channel VI or the DAQmx Create Task VI.
- [DAQmx Unflatten Channel String VI](../../../../vi-lib/daqmx/miscellaneous-llb/daqmx-unflatten-channel-string-vi.html) Converts a comma-delimited list or range of physical or virtual channels into an array of physical or virtual channel names.

<!--NI_TOPIC bundle=ni-daqmx-labview-api-ref path=menus/categories/measurement/daqmx/calib-mnu.html language=enus -->
## TOPIC 00525: DAQmx Calibration

- bundle_id: `ni-daqmx-labview-api-ref`
- source_path: `menus/categories/measurement/daqmx/calib-mnu.html`
- source_url: https://docs-be.ni.com/bundle/ni-daqmx-labview-api-ref/raw/resource/enus/menus/categories/measurement/daqmx/calib-mnu.html
- document_id: `ni-daqmx-labview-api-ref`
- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: `reference`
- source_description: Use the DAQmx Calibration VIs and functions to perform internal and external calibration of devices. icon

### DAQmx Calibration

Use the DAQmx Calibration VIs and functions to perform internal and external calibration of devices.

[IMAGE alt='icon' src='calib-mnu.png']

- [DAQmx Self Calibrate VI](../../../../vi-lib/daqmx/calibration/calibrationinfo-llb/daqmx-self-calibrate-vi.html) Measures the onboard reference voltage of the device and adjusts the self-calibration constants to account for any errors caused by short-term fluctuations in the operating environment. When you self-calibrate a device, no external signal connections are necessary.
- [DAQmx Perform Bridge Offset Nulling Calibration VI](../../../../vi-lib/daqmx/calibration/calibrationinfo-llb/daqmx-perform-bridge-offset-nulling-calibration-vi.html) Performs a bridge offset nulling calibration on the channels in the task. If the task measures both bridge-based sensors and non-bridge-based sensors, use the channels input to specify the names of the channels that measure bridge-based sensors.
- [DAQmx Perform Shunt Calibration VI](../../../../vi-lib/daqmx/calibration/calibrationinfo-llb/daqmx-perform-shunt-calibration-vi.html) Performs shunt calibration for the specified channels of the task. The instances of this polymorphic VI correspond to the type of bridge sensor. Refer to the calibration procedure for your module for detailed calibration instructions.
- [DAQmx Perform Thermocouple Lead Offset Nulling Calibration VI](../../../../vi-lib/daqmx/calibration/calibrationinfo-llb/daqmx-perform-thermocouple-lead-offset-nulling-calibration-vi.html) Performs thermocouple lead offset nulling calibration on the channels in the task to compensate for offsets introduced by open thermocouple detection.
- [DAQmx Calibration Info Property Node](../../../../vi-lib/daqmx/calibration/calibrationinfo-llb/daqmx-calibration-info-property-node-vi.html) A Property Node with the DAQmx Calibration Info class preselected. Right-click the Property Node and choose Select Filter from the shortcut menu to make the Property Node show only the properties supported by a particular device installed in the system or supported by all the devices installed in the system.
- [DAQmx Restore Last External Calibration Constants VI](../../../../vi-lib/daqmx/calibration/calibrationinfo-llb/daqmx-restore-last-external-calibration-constants-vi.html) Sets the self-calibration constants of the device to the external calibration constants. NI sets the external calibration constants at the factory, and those constants remain in effect until you perform a new external calibration on the device.
- [DAQmx Change External Calibration Password VI](../../../../vi-lib/daqmx/calibration/calibrationinfo-llb/daqmx-change-external-calibration-password-vi.html) Changes the external calibration password of the device.
- [DAQmx Initialize External Calibration VI](../../../../vi-lib/daqmx/calibration/calibrationinfo-llb/daqmx-initialize-external-calibration-vi.html) Starts an external calibration session on a device.
- [DAQmx Close External Calibration VI](../../../../vi-lib/daqmx/calibration/calibrationinfo-llb/daqmx-close-external-calibration-vi.html) Closes an open external calibration session.
- [DAQmx Adjust 64xx Calibration VI](../../../../vi-lib/daqmx/calibration/calibrationinfo-llb/daqmx-adjust-64xx-calibration-vi.html) Adjusts the external calibration constants for a 64xx Series device. You must connect a known voltage to the device and specify that voltage with reference voltage .
- [DAQmx Adjust E-Series Calibration VI](../../../../vi-lib/daqmx/calibration/calibrationinfo-llb/daqmx-adjust-e-series-calibration-vi.html) Adjusts the external calibration constants for an E Series device. You must connect a known voltage to the device and specify that voltage with reference voltage .
- [DAQmx Adjust AO-Series Calibration VI](../../../../vi-lib/daqmx/calibration/calibrationinfo-llb/daqmx-adjust-ao-series-calibration-vi.html) Adjusts the external calibration constants for an AO Series device. You must connect a known voltage to the device and specify that voltage with reference voltage .
- [DAQmx Adjust S-Series Calibration VI](../../../../vi-lib/daqmx/calibration/calibrationinfo-llb/daqmx-adjust-s-series-calibration-vi.html) Adjusts the external calibration constants for an S Series device. You must connect a known voltage to the device and specify that voltage with reference voltage .
- [DAQmx Adjust M-Series Calibration VI](../../../../vi-lib/daqmx/calibration/calibrationinfo-llb/daqmx-adjust-m-series-calibration-vi.html) Adjusts the external calibration constants for an M Series device. You must connect a known voltage to the device and specify that voltage with reference voltage .
- [DAQmx Adjust X Series Calibration VI](../../../../vi-lib/daqmx/calibration/calibrationinfo-llb/daqmx-adjust-x-series-calibration-vi.html) Adjusts the external calibration constants for an X Series device. You must connect a known voltage to the device and specify that voltage with reference voltage .
- [DAQmx DSA Calibration](../../../../menus/categories/measurement/daqmx/calibdsa-mnu.html) Use the DAQmx DSA Calibration VIs to perform external calibrations of the analog input section, analog output section, and timebase of DSA devices.
- [DAQmx 42xx Calibration](../../../../menus/categories/measurement/daqmx/calib42xx-mnu.html) Use the DAQmx 42xx Calibration VIs to calibrate NI 42xx devices.
- [DAQmx SCXI Calibration](../../../../menus/categories/measurement/daqmx/calibscxi-mnu.html) Use the DAQmx SCXI Calibration VIs to perform external calibrations of SCXI modules.
- [DAQmx SC Express Calibration](../../../../menus/categories/measurement/daqmx/calibscexpress-mnu.html) Use the DAQmx SC Express Calibration VIs to perform external calibrations of SC Express devices.
- [DAQmx C Series Calibration](../../../../menus/categories/measurement/daqmx/calibcseries-mnu.html) Use the DAQmx C Series Calibration VIs to perform external calibrations of C Series devices.
- [DAQmx TIO Calibration](../../../../menus/categories/measurement/daqmx/calibtio-mnu.html) Use the DAQmx TIO Calibration VIs to perform external calibrations of TIO devices.
- [DAQmx FieldDAQ Calibration](../../../../menus/categories/measurement/daqmx/calibfielddaq-mnu.html) Use the DAQmx FieldDAQ Calibration VIs to perform external calibrations of FieldDAQ devices.
- [TS Cal](../../../../menus/categories/measurement/daqmx/calibtsexpress-mnu.html) Use these VIs and functions to perform internal and external calibration of NI TestScale devices.

Parent topic:

DAQmx Advanced

<!--NI_TOPIC bundle=ni-daqmx-labview-api-ref path=menus/categories/measurement/daqmx/calib42xx-mnu.html language=enus -->
## TOPIC 00526: DAQmx 42xx Calibration

- bundle_id: `ni-daqmx-labview-api-ref`
- source_path: `menus/categories/measurement/daqmx/calib42xx-mnu.html`
- source_url: https://docs-be.ni.com/bundle/ni-daqmx-labview-api-ref/raw/resource/enus/menus/categories/measurement/daqmx/calib42xx-mnu.html
- document_id: `ni-daqmx-labview-api-ref`
- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: `reference`
- source_description: Use the DAQmx 42xx Calibration VIs to calibrate NI 42xx devices. icon

### DAQmx 42xx Calibration

Use the DAQmx 42xx Calibration VIs to calibrate NI 42xx devices.

[IMAGE alt='icon' src='calib42xx-mnu.png']

- [DAQmx Adjust 4204 Calibration VI](../../../../vi-lib/daqmx/calibration/calibrationinfo-llb/daqmx-adjust-4204-calibration-vi.html) Adjusts the internal and external calibration constants for an NI 4204 device. You must connect a known voltage to the device and specify that voltage with reference voltage .
- [DAQmx Adjust 4220 Calibration VI](../../../../vi-lib/daqmx/calibration/calibrationinfo-llb/daqmx-adjust-4220-calibration-vi.html) Adjusts the internal and external calibration constants for an NI 4220 device. This device requires reference signals of 0.0 volts at gains of 1, 15, 20, and 310 on a particular channel in order to perform an offset calibration for that channel. If you do not manually supply those reference signals, the device measures them internally with sample and hold circuitry enabled.
- [DAQmx Adjust 4224 Calibration VI](../../../../vi-lib/daqmx/calibration/calibrationinfo-llb/daqmx-adjust-4224-calibration-vi.html) Adjusts the internal and external calibration constants for an NI 4224 device. You must connect a known voltage to the device and specify that voltage with reference voltage .
- [DAQmx Adjust SC Baseboard Calibration VI](../../../../vi-lib/daqmx/calibration/calibrationinfo-llb/daqmx-adjust-sc-baseboard-calibration-vi.html) Adjusts the external calibration constants for the baseboard of an SC Series device. You must connect a known voltage to the device and specify that voltage with reference voltage .

Parent topic:

DAQmx Calibration

- [DAQmx Get C Series Calibration Adjustment Points VI](../../../../vi-lib/daqmx/calibration/calibrationinfo-llb/daqmx-get-c-series-calibration-adjustment-points-vi.html) Returns the reference values to pass to DAQmx Adjust C Series Calibration. The instances of this polymorphic VI correspond to the model of the device you want to calibrate. Refer to the calibration procedure for your device for detailed calibration instructions.

- [DAQmx Set Temperature C Series Calibration VI](../../../../vi-lib/daqmx/calibration/calibrationinfo-llb/daqmx-set-temperature-c-series-calibration-vi.html) Specifies the temperature of a C Series device for the current external calibration session.

## TOPIC 00530: DAQmx SC Express Calibration

- bundle_id: `ni-daqmx-labview-api-ref`
- source_path: `menus/categories/measurement/daqmx/calibscexpress-mnu.html`
- source_url: https://docs-be.ni.com/bundle/ni-daqmx-labview-api-ref/raw/resource/enus/menus/categories/measurement/daqmx/calibscexpress-mnu.html
- document_id: `ni-daqmx-labview-api-ref`
- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: `reference`
- source_description: Use the DAQmx SC Express Calibration VIs to perform external calibrations of SC Express devices. icon

### DAQmx SC Express Calibration

Use the DAQmx SC Express Calibration VIs to perform external calibrations of SC Express devices.

[IMAGE alt='icon' src='calibscexpress-mnu.png']

- [DAQmx Get SC Express Calibration Adjustment Points VI](../../../../vi-lib/daqmx/calibration/calibrationinfo-llb/daqmx-get-sc-express-calibration-adjustment-points-vi.html) Returns the reference values to pass to DAQmx Adjust SC Express Calibration. The instances of this polymorphic VI correspond to the model of the device you want to calibrate. Refer to the calibration procedure for your device for detailed calibration instructions.
- [DAQmx Setup SC Express Calibration VI](../../../../vi-lib/daqmx/calibration/calibrationinfo-llb/daqmx-setup-sc-express-calibration-vi.html) Sets up calibration for SC Express devices. The instances of this polymorphic VI correspond to the model of the device you want to calibrate. Refer to the calibration procedure for your device for detailed calibration instructions.
- [DAQmx Adjust SC Express Calibration VI](../../../../vi-lib/daqmx/calibration/calibrationinfo-llb/daqmx-adjust-sc-express-calibration-vi.html) Adjusts the external calibration constants for an SC Express device. The instances of this polymorphic VI correspond to the model of the device you want to calibrate. Refer to the calibration procedure for your device for detailed calibration instructions.
- [DAQmx Connect SC Express Calibration Accessory Channels VI](../../../../vi-lib/daqmx/calibration/calibrationinfo-llb/daqmx-connect-sc-express-calibration-accessory-channels-vi.html) Configures a connection on the SC Express accessory for the specified physical channel(s).
- [DAQmx Disconnect SC Express Calibration Accessory Channels VI](../../../../vi-lib/daqmx/calibration/calibrationinfo-llb/daqmx-disconnect-sc-express-calibration-accessory-channels-vi.html) Disconnects the configured connection on an SC Express accessory and connects the accessory in the default configuration.
- [DAQmx Get Possible SC Express Calibration Accessory Connections VI](../../../../vi-lib/daqmx/calibration/calibrationinfo-llb/daqmx-get-possible-sc-express-calibration-accessory-connections-vi.html) Gets the available connections on an SC Express accessory for the specified physical channel(s). Connections specify how channels on the SC Express accessory should be configured. The resulting configuration could connect channels to a particular external signal or an onboard terminal.
- [DAQmx Set SC Express Calibration Accessory Bridge Output VI](../../../../vi-lib/daqmx/calibration/calibrationinfo-llb/daqmx-set-sc-express-calibration-accessory-bridge-output-vi.html) Configures an SC Express accessory to produce the bridge output specified in volts-per-volt.

Parent topic:

DAQmx Calibration

- [DAQmx Get TS Series Calibration Adjustment Points VI](../../../../vi-lib/daqmx/calibration/calibrationinfo-llb/daqmx-get-ts-series-calibration-adjustment-points-vi.html) Returns the DAC or reference values with which to configure the device under calibration.

## TOPIC 00534: DAQmx cDAQ Sync

- bundle_id: `ni-daqmx-labview-api-ref`
- source_path: `menus/categories/measurement/daqmx/cdaqsync-mnu.html`
- source_url: https://docs-be.ni.com/bundle/ni-daqmx-labview-api-ref/raw/resource/enus/menus/categories/measurement/daqmx/cdaqsync-mnu.html
- document_id: `ni-daqmx-labview-api-ref`
- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: `reference`
- source_description: Use the DAQmx cDAQ Sync VIs and functions to set up and configure cDAQ Sync devices. icon

### DAQmx cDAQ Sync

Use the DAQmx cDAQ Sync VIs and functions to set up and configure cDAQ Sync devices.

[IMAGE alt='icon' src='cdaqsync-mnu.png']

- [DAQmx Auto-Configure cDAQ Sync Connections VI](../../../../vi-lib/daqmx/configure/system-llb/daqmx-auto-configure-cdaq-sync-connections-vi.html) Detects and configures cDAQ Sync connections between devices. Stop all NI-DAQmx tasks running on the devices prior to running this VI because any running tasks cause auto-configuration to fail.
- [DAQmx Are Configured cDAQ Sync Ports Disconnected VI](../../../../vi-lib/daqmx/configure/system-llb/daqmx-are-configured-cdaq-sync-ports-disconnected-vi.html) Verifies configured cDAQ Sync connections between devices. Failures generally indicate a wiring issue or that a device has been powered off or removed. Stop all NI-DAQmx tasks running on the devices prior to running this VI because any running tasks cause the verification process to fail.
- [DAQmx Add cDAQ Sync Connection VI](../../../../vi-lib/daqmx/configure/system-llb/daqmx-add-cdaq-sync-connection-vi.html) Adds a cDAQ Sync connection between devices. The connection is not verified.
- [DAQmx Remove cDAQ Sync Connection VI](../../../../vi-lib/daqmx/configure/system-llb/daqmx-remove-cdaq-sync-connection-vi.html) Removes a cDAQ Sync connection between devices. The connection is not verified.

Parent topic:

DAQmx System Setup

## TOPIC 00535: DAQmx Export Signal

- bundle_id: `ni-daqmx-labview-api-ref`
- source_path: `menus/categories/measurement/daqmx/eventrtg-mnu.html`
- source_url: https://docs-be.ni.com/bundle/ni-daqmx-labview-api-ref/raw/resource/enus/menus/categories/measurement/daqmx/eventrtg-mnu.html
- document_id: `ni-daqmx-labview-api-ref`
- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: `reference`
- source_description: Use the DAQmx Export Signal VI and functions to configure and route control signals within a device or from one device to another. icon

### DAQmx Export Signal

Use the DAQmx Export Signal VI and functions to configure and route control signals within a device or from one device to another.

[IMAGE alt='icon' src='eventrtg-mnu.png']

- [DAQmx Export Signal VI](../../../../vi-lib/daqmx/configure/events/hardwaresignals-llb/daqmx-export-signal-vi.html) Routes a control signal to the terminal you specify. The output terminal can reside on the device that generates the control signal or on a different device. You can use this VI to share clocks and triggers among multiple tasks and devices. The routes this VI creates are task-based routes.
- [DAQmx Export Signal Property Node](../../../../vi-lib/daqmx/configure/events/hardwaresignals-llb/daqmx-export-signal-property-node-vi.html) A Property Node with the DAQmx Export Signal class preselected. Right-click the Property Node and choose Select Filter from the shortcut menu to make the Property Node show only the properties supported by a particular device installed in the system or supported by all the devices installed in the system.
- [DAQmx Terminal](../../../../constants/daqmx-terminal.html) Lists all terminals available on devices installed in the system. Select Browse to select multiple terminals. Right-click the constant and select I/O Name Filtering from the shortcut menu to limit the terminals that the constant displays and to limit what you can enter in the constant.

Parent topic:

DAQmx Advanced Task Options

### DAQmx Events

- [DAQmx Create Event VI](../../../../vi-lib/daqmx/miscellaneous-llb/daqmx-create-event-vi.html) Contains a Register for Events function, an Event structure , and a DAQmx Task Name constant . You must register the DAQmx event you want to use and configure the Event structure to handle that event. You must also use the DAQmx Task Name constant to select or create a task. You can use a DAQmx Task Name control in place of the constant.

## TOPIC 00537: DAQmx Device Configuration

- bundle_id: `ni-daqmx-labview-api-ref`
- source_path: `menus/categories/measurement/daqmx/hwspc-mnu.html`
- source_url: https://docs-be.ni.com/bundle/ni-daqmx-labview-api-ref/raw/resource/enus/menus/categories/measurement/daqmx/hwspc-mnu.html
- document_id: `ni-daqmx-labview-api-ref`
- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: `reference`
- source_description: Use the DAQmx Device Configuration VIs and functions for hardware-specific configuration and control. icon

### DAQmx Device Configuration

Use the DAQmx Device Configuration VIs and functions for hardware-specific configuration and control.

[IMAGE alt='icon' src='hwspc-mnu.png']

- [DAQmx Watchdog](../../../../menus/categories/measurement/daqmx/watchdog-mnu.html) Use the DAQmx Watchdog VIs and function to configure and control the watchdog timer of a device.
- [DAQmx Reset Device VI](../../../../vi-lib/daqmx/configure/system-llb/daqmx-reset-device-vi.html) Immediately aborts all active tasks associated with a device, disconnects any routes, and returns the device to an initialized state. Aborting a task immediately terminates the currently active operation, such as a read or a write. Aborting a task puts the task into an unstable but recoverable state. To recover the task, use DAQmx Start to restart the task or use DAQmx Stop to reset the task without starting it.
- [DAQmx Self-Test Device VI](../../../../vi-lib/daqmx/configure/system-llb/daqmx-self-test-device-vi.html) Performs a brief test of device resources. If a failure occurs, refer to your device documentation for more information.

Parent topic:

DAQmx - Data Acquisition

## TOPIC 00538: DAQmx Constants & Property Nodes

- bundle_id: `ni-daqmx-labview-api-ref`
- source_path: `menus/categories/measurement/daqmx/ioconstants-mnu.html`
- source_url: https://docs-be.ni.com/bundle/ni-daqmx-labview-api-ref/raw/resource/enus/menus/categories/measurement/daqmx/ioconstants-mnu.html
- document_id: `ni-daqmx-labview-api-ref`
- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: `reference`
- source_description: The DAQmx Constants and Property Nodes palette contains all I/O constants and property nodes used in NI-DAQmx icon

### DAQmx Constants & Property Nodes

The DAQmx Constants and Property Nodes palette contains all I/O constants and property nodes used in NI-DAQmx

[IMAGE alt='icon' src='ioconstants-mnu.png']

- [DAQmx Scale Name](../../../../constants/daqmx-scale-name.html) Lists all custom scales you create and save by using the DAQ Assistant . Right-click the constant, and select I/O Name Filtering from the shortcut menu to limit the scales that the constant displays and to limit what you can enter in the constant.
- [DAQmx Physical Channel](../../../../constants/daqmx-physical-channel.html) Lists all physical channels on devices installed in the system. Select Browse to select multiple physical channels. Right-click the constant, and select I/O Name Filtering from the shortcut menu to limit the physical channels that the constant displays and to limit what you can enter in the constant.
- [DAQmx Physical Channel Property Node](../../../../vi-lib/daqmx/configure/channels-llb/daqmx-physical-channel-property-node-vi.html) A Property Node with the DAQmx Physical Channel class preselected. Right-click the Property Node and choose Select Filter from the shortcut menu to make the Property Node show only the properties supported by a particular device installed in the system or supported by all the devices installed in the system.
- [DAQmx Task Name](../../../../constants/daqmx-task-name.html) Lists all tasks you create and save by using the DAQ Assistant . You cannot use this constant to select multiple tasks. Right-click the constant, and select I/O Name Filtering from the shortcut menu to limit the tasks that the constant displays and to limit what you can enter in the constant.
- [DAQmx Global Channel](../../../../constants/daqmx-global-channel.html) Lists all virtual channels you create and save using the DAQ Assistant . Select Browse to select multiple channels. Right-click the constant and select I/O Name Filtering from the shortcut menu to limit the channels that the constant displays and to limit what you can enter in the constant.
- [DAQmx Terminal](../../../../constants/daqmx-terminal.html) Lists all terminals available on devices installed in the system. Select Browse to select multiple terminals. Right-click the constant and select I/O Name Filtering from the shortcut menu to limit the terminals that the constant displays and to limit what you can enter in the constant.
- [DAQmx Device Name](../../../../constants/daqmx-device-name.html) Lists all devices installed in the system. Right-click the constant, and select I/O Name Filtering from the shortcut menu to limit the devices that the constant displays and to limit what you can enter in the constant. If you right-click this constant and create a Property Node, the Property Node is for the constant itself and is not a DAQmx Device Property Node.
- [DAQmx Task Property Node](../../../../vi-lib/daqmx/configure/task-llb/daqmx-task-property-node-vi.html) A Property Node with the DAQmx Task class preselected. Right-click the Property Node and choose Select Filter from the shortcut menu to make the Property Node show only the properties supported by a particular device installed in the system or supported by all the devices installed in the system.
- [DAQmx Channel Property Node](../../../../vi-lib/daqmx/configure/channels-llb/daqmx-channel-property-node-vi.html) A Property Node with the DAQmx Channel class preselected. Right-click the Property Node and choose Select Filter from the shortcut menu to make the Property Node show only the properties supported by a particular device installed in the system or supported by all devices installed in the system.
- [DAQmx Timing Property Node](../../../../vi-lib/daqmx/configure/timing-llb/daqmx-timing-property-node-vi.html) A Property Node with the DAQmx Timing class preselected. Right-click the Property Node and choose Select Filter from the shortcut menu to make the Property Node show only the properties supported by a particular device installed in the system or supported by all the devices installed in the system.
- [DAQmx Trigger Property Node](../../../../vi-lib/daqmx/configure/trigger-llb/daqmx-trigger-property-node-vi.html) A Property Node with the DAQmx Trigger class preselected. Right-click the Property Node and choose Select Filter from the shortcut menu to make the Property Node show only the properties supported by a particular device installed in the system or supported by all the devices installed in the system.
- [DAQmx Read Property Node](../../../../vi-lib/daqmx/read-llb/daqmx-read-property-node-vi.html) A Property Node with the DAQmx Read class preselected. Right-click the Property Node and choose Select Filter from the shortcut menu to make the Property Node show only the properties supported by a particular device installed in the system or supported by all the devices installed in the system.
- [DAQmx Write Property Node](../../../../vi-lib/daqmx/write-llb/daqmx-write-property-node-vi.html) A Property Node with the DAQmx Write class preselected. Right-click the Property Node and choose Select Filter from the shortcut menu to make the Property Node show only the properties supported by a particular device installed in the system or supported by all the devices installed in the system.
- [DAQmx Timing Source Property Node](../../../../vi-lib/daqmx/configure/timing-llb/daqmx-timing-source-property-node-vi.html) A Property Node with the DAQmx Timing Source class preselected. Right-click the Property Node and choose Select Filter from the shortcut menu to make the Property Node show only the properties supported by a particular device installed in the system or supported by all the devices installed in the system.
- [DAQmx Buffer Property Node](../../../../vi-lib/daqmx/configure/buffer-llb/daqmx-buffer-property-node-vi.html) A Property Node with the DAQmx Buffer class preselected. Right-click the Property Node and choose Select Filter from the shortcut menu to make the Property Node show only the properties supported by a particular device installed in the system or supported by all the devices installed in the system.
- [DAQmx Real-Time Property Node](../../../../vi-lib/daqmx/configure/timing-llb/daqmx-real-time-property-node-vi.html) A Property Node with the DAQmx Real-Time class preselected. Right-click the Property Node and choose Select Filter from the shortcut menu to make the Property Node show only the properties supported by a particular device installed in the system or supported by all the devices installed in the system.
- [DAQmx System Property Node](../../../../vi-lib/daqmx/configure/system-llb/daqmx-system-property-node-vi.html) A Property Node with the DAQmx System class preselected. Right-click the Property Node and choose Select Filter from the shortcut menu to make the Property Node show only the properties supported by a particular device installed in the system or supported by all the devices installed in the system.
- [DAQmx Device Property Node](../../../../vi-lib/daqmx/configure/system-llb/daqmx-device-property-node-vi.html) A Property Node with the DAQmx Device class preselected. Right-click the Property Node and choose Select Filter from the shortcut menu to make the Property Node show only the properties supported by a particular device installed in the system or supported by all the devices installed in the system.

Right-click the Property Node and choose Select Filter from the shortcut menu to make the Property Node show only the properties supported by a particular device installed in the system or supported by all the devices installed in the system.

Right-click the Property Node and choose Select Filter from the shortcut menu to make the Property Node show only the properties supported by a particular device installed in the system or supported by all the devices installed in the system.
- [DAQmx Calibration Info Property Node](../../../../vi-lib/daqmx/calibration/calibrationinfo-llb/daqmx-calibration-info-property-node-vi.html) A Property Node with the DAQmx Calibration Info class preselected. Right-click the Property Node and choose Select Filter from the shortcut menu to make the Property Node show only the properties supported by a particular device installed in the system or supported by all the devices installed in the system.

Right-click the Property Node and choose Select Filter from the shortcut menu to make the Property Node show only the properties supported by a particular device installed in the system or supported by all devices installed in the system.

## TOPIC 00539: DAQmx Scale Setup

- bundle_id: `ni-daqmx-labview-api-ref`
- source_path: `menus/categories/measurement/daqmx/progcreation-mnu.html`
- source_url: https://docs-be.ni.com/bundle/ni-daqmx-labview-api-ref/raw/resource/enus/menus/categories/measurement/daqmx/progcreation-mnu.html
- document_id: `ni-daqmx-labview-api-ref`
- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: `reference`
- source_description: Use the DAQmx Scale Setup VIs and property nodes for custom scale creation and configuration. icon

### DAQmx Scale Setup

Use the DAQmx Scale Setup VIs and property nodes for custom scale creation and configuration.

[IMAGE alt='icon' src='progcreation-mnu.png']

- [DAQmx Create Scale VI](../../../../vi-lib/daqmx/create/scale-llb/daqmx-create-scale-vi.html) Creates and configures a custom scale . Apply custom scales to input and output channels to provide additional scaling. The instances of this polymorphic VI correspond to the type of scale this VI creates.
- [DAQmx Scale Property Node](../../../../vi-lib/daqmx/configure/scales-llb/daqmx-scale-property-node-vi.html) A Property Node with the DAQmx Scale class preselected. Right-click the Property Node and choose Select Filter from the shortcut menu to make the Property Node show only the properties supported by a particular device installed in the system or supported by all the devices installed in the system.
- [DAQmx Compute Reverse Polynomial Coefficients VI](../../../../vi-lib/daqmx/miscellaneous-llb/daqmx-compute-reverse-polynomial-coefficients-vi.html) Computes a set of coefficients for a polynomial that approximates the inverse of the polynomial with the coefficients you specify with the coefficients input. This VI generates a table of x versus y values over the range of x . This VI then finds a polynomial fit, using the least squares method to compute a polynomial that computes x when given a value for y .

Parent topic:

DAQmx Advanced

<!--NI_TOPIC bundle=ni-daqmx-labview-api-ref path=menus/categories/measurement/daqmx/realtime-mnu.html language=enus -->
## TOPIC 00540: DAQmx Real-Time

- bundle_id: `ni-daqmx-labview-api-ref`
- source_path: `menus/categories/measurement/daqmx/realtime-mnu.html`
- source_url: https://docs-be.ni.com/bundle/ni-daqmx-labview-api-ref/raw/resource/enus/menus/categories/measurement/daqmx/realtime-mnu.html
- document_id: `ni-daqmx-labview-api-ref`
- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: `reference`
- source_description: Use the DAQmx Real Time VIs and function to configure and perform real-time operations. icon

### DAQmx Real-Time

Use the DAQmx Real Time VIs and function to configure and perform real-time operations.

[IMAGE alt='icon' src='realtime-mnu.png']

- [DAQmx Wait For Next Sample Clock VI](../../../../vi-lib/daqmx/configure/timing-llb/daqmx-wait-for-next-sample-clock-vi.html) Waits until the next pulse of the Sample Clock occurs. If an extra Sample Clock pulse occurs between calls to this VI, the second call returns an error or warning and waits for the next Sample Clock pulse. Use the Convert Late Errors to Warnings DAQmx Real-Time property to specify whether this VI returns errors or warnings. If that property is TRUE, any warnings this VI returns do not include the source string.
- [DAQmx Real-Time Property Node](../../../../vi-lib/daqmx/configure/timing-llb/daqmx-real-time-property-node-vi.html) A Property Node with the DAQmx Real-Time class preselected. Right-click the Property Node and choose Select Filter from the shortcut menu to make the Property Node show only the properties supported by a particular device installed in the system or supported by all the devices installed in the system.
- [Timed Loop](../../../../menus/categories/measurement/daqmx/timedloop-mnu.html) Use the DAQmx Timed Loop VI and function to create and configure timing sources for Timed Loops.

Parent topic:

DAQmx - Data Acquisition

<!--NI_TOPIC bundle=ni-daqmx-labview-api-ref path=menus/categories/measurement/daqmx/storage-mnu.html language=enus -->
## TOPIC 00541: DAQmx Storage

- bundle_id: `ni-daqmx-labview-api-ref`
- source_path: `menus/categories/measurement/daqmx/storage-mnu.html`
- source_url: https://docs-be.ni.com/bundle/ni-daqmx-labview-api-ref/raw/resource/enus/menus/categories/measurement/daqmx/storage-mnu.html
- document_id: `ni-daqmx-labview-api-ref`
- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: `reference`
- source_description: Use the DAQmx Storage VIs and functions to save and delete tasks, global channels, and custom scales in MAX. icon

### DAQmx Storage

Use the DAQmx Storage VIs and functions to save and delete tasks, global channels, and custom scales in MAX.

[IMAGE alt='icon' src='storage-mnu.png']

- [DAQmx Save Task VI](../../../../vi-lib/daqmx/configure/storage-llb/daqmx-save-task-vi.html) Saves the specified task and any local channels it contains to MAX. This VI does not save global channels. Use the DAQmx Save Global Channel VI to save global channels.
- [DAQmx Save Global Channel VI](../../../../vi-lib/daqmx/configure/storage-llb/daqmx-save-global-channel-vi.html) Saves the specified local or global channel to MAX as a global channel. You must specify both the local or global channel to save and a task that contains that channel.
- [DAQmx Save Scale VI](../../../../vi-lib/daqmx/configure/storage-llb/daqmx-save-scale-vi.html) Saves the specified custom scale to MAX.
- [DAQmx Delete Saved Task VI](../../../../vi-lib/daqmx/configure/storage-llb/daqmx-delete-saved-task-vi.html) Deletes the specified task from MAX. This VI does not clear the copy of the task stored in memory. Use the DAQmx Clear Task VI to clear that copy of the task.
- [DAQmx Delete Saved Global Channel VI](../../../../vi-lib/daqmx/configure/storage-llb/daqmx-delete-saved-global-channel-vi.html) Deletes the specified global channel from MAX. This VI does not remove the global channel from tasks that use it.
- [DAQmx Delete Saved Scale VI](../../../../vi-lib/daqmx/configure/storage-llb/daqmx-delete-saved-scale-vi.html) Deletes the specified custom scale from MAX. This VI does not remove the custom scale from virtual channels that use it.
- [DAQmx Persisted Task Property Node](../../../../vi-lib/daqmx/configure/storage-llb/daqmx-persisted-task-property-node-vi.html) A Property Node with the DAQmx Persisted Task class preselected. Right-click the Property Node and choose Select Filter from the shortcut menu to make the Property Node show only the properties supported by a particular device installed in the system or supported by all the devices installed in the system.
- [DAQmx Persisted Channel Property Node](../../../../vi-lib/daqmx/configure/storage-llb/daqmx-persisted-channel-property-node-vi.html) A Property Node with the DAQmx Persisted Channel class preselected. Right-click the Property Node and choose Select Filter from the shortcut menu to make the Property Node show only the properties supported by a particular device installed in the system or supported by all the devices installed in the system.
- [DAQmx Persisted Scale Property Node](../../../../vi-lib/daqmx/configure/storage-llb/daqmx-persisted-scale-property-node-vi.html) A Property Node with the DAQmx Persisted Scale class preselected. Right-click the Property Node and choose Select Filter from the shortcut menu to make the Property Node show only the properties supported by a particular device installed in the system or supported by all the devices installed in the system.

Parent topic:

DAQmx System Setup

<!--NI_TOPIC bundle=ni-daqmx-labview-api-ref path=menus/categories/measurement/daqmx/syscfg-mnu.html language=enus -->
## TOPIC 00542: DAQmx System Setup

- bundle_id: `ni-daqmx-labview-api-ref`
- source_path: `menus/categories/measurement/daqmx/syscfg-mnu.html`
- source_url: https://docs-be.ni.com/bundle/ni-daqmx-labview-api-ref/raw/resource/enus/menus/categories/measurement/daqmx/syscfg-mnu.html
- document_id: `ni-daqmx-labview-api-ref`
- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: `reference`
- source_description: Use the DAQmx System Setup functions to query information about your devices and software configuration from Measurement & Automation Explorer. icon

### DAQmx System Setup

Use the DAQmx System Setup functions to query information about your devices and software configuration from Measurement & Automation Explorer.

[IMAGE alt='icon' src='syscfg-mnu.png']

- [DAQmx Device Name](../../../../constants/daqmx-device-name.html) Lists all devices installed in the system. Right-click the constant, and select I/O Name Filtering from the shortcut menu to limit the devices that the constant displays and to limit what you can enter in the constant. If you right-click this constant and create a Property Node, the Property Node is for the constant itself and is not a DAQmx Device Property Node.
- [DAQmx System Property Node](../../../../vi-lib/daqmx/configure/system-llb/daqmx-system-property-node-vi.html) A Property Node with the DAQmx System class preselected. Right-click the Property Node and choose Select Filter from the shortcut menu to make the Property Node show only the properties supported by a particular device installed in the system or supported by all the devices installed in the system.
- [DAQmx Device Property Node](../../../../vi-lib/daqmx/configure/system-llb/daqmx-device-property-node-vi.html) A Property Node with the DAQmx Device class preselected. Right-click the Property Node and choose Select Filter from the shortcut menu to make the Property Node show only the properties supported by a particular device installed in the system or supported by all the devices installed in the system.
- [DAQmx Set Power Up States VI](../../../../vi-lib/daqmx/configure/system-llb/daqmx-set-power-up-states-vi.html) Updates the states to which to set physical channels on a device when the device powers up or when you reset the device. A device stores power up states in non-volatile memory that you can write to only a limited number of times. Therefore, you should use this VI as infrequently as possible. This VI writes to the non-volatile memory only if a setting you request is different from the one currently stored. This VI writes power up states in the sequential order of the power up states array. Therefore, any physical channels with multiple entries in that array use the highest array index.
- [DAQmx Get Power Up States VI](../../../../vi-lib/daqmx/configure/system-llb/daqmx-get-power-up-states-vi.html) Returns the power up states that physical channels on a device are set to when the device powers up or when you reset the device. This VI returns data for only one line.
- [DAQmx Write ID Pin Memory VI](../../../../vi-lib/daqmx/configure/system-llb/daqmx-write-id-pin-memory-vi.html) Writes the supplied data and format code to the EEPROM connected to the specified ID pin.
- [DAQmx Read ID Pin Memory VI](../../../../vi-lib/daqmx/configure/system-llb/daqmx-read-id-pin-memory-vi.html) Reads and returns the data and format code stored in the memory attached to the specified ID Pin.
- [DAQmx Add Network Device VI](../../../../vi-lib/daqmx/configure/system-llb/daqmx-add-network-device-vi.html) Adds a Network cDAQ device to the system and, if specified, attempts to reserve it.
- [DAQmx Delete Network Device VI](../../../../vi-lib/daqmx/configure/system-llb/daqmx-delete-network-device-vi.html) Deletes a Network DAQ device previously added to the host. If the device is reserved, it is unreserved before it is removed.
- [DAQmx Reserve Network Device VI](../../../../vi-lib/daqmx/configure/system-llb/daqmx-reserve-network-device-vi.html) Reserves the Network DAQ device for the current host. Reservation is required to run NI-DAQmx tasks, and the device must be added in MAX before it can be reserved.
- [DAQmx Unreserve Network Device VI](../../../../vi-lib/daqmx/configure/system-llb/daqmx-unreserve-network-device-vi.html) Unreserves or releases a Network DAQ device previously reserved by the host.
- [DAQmx Storage](../../../../menus/categories/measurement/daqmx/storage-mnu.html) Use the DAQmx Storage VIs and functions to save and delete tasks, global channels, and custom scales in MAX.
- [DAQmx cDAQ Sync](../../../../menus/categories/measurement/daqmx/cdaqsync-mnu.html) Use the DAQmx cDAQ Sync VIs and functions to set up and configure cDAQ Sync devices.

Parent topic:

DAQmx Advanced

<!--NI_TOPIC bundle=ni-daqmx-labview-api-ref path=menus/categories/measurement/daqmx/teds-mnu.html language=enus -->
## TOPIC 00543: DAQmx TEDS

- bundle_id: `ni-daqmx-labview-api-ref`
- source_path: `menus/categories/measurement/daqmx/teds-mnu.html`
- source_url: https://docs-be.ni.com/bundle/ni-daqmx-labview-api-ref/raw/resource/enus/menus/categories/measurement/daqmx/teds-mnu.html
- document_id: `ni-daqmx-labview-api-ref`
- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: `reference`
- source_description: Use the DAQmx TEDS VIs and function to configure physical channels to use and to retrieve TEDS information from a physical channel. icon

### DAQmx TEDS

Use the DAQmx TEDS VIs and function to configure physical channels to use and to retrieve TEDS information from a physical channel.

[IMAGE alt='icon' src='teds-mnu.png']

- [DAQmx Configure TEDS VI](../../../../vi-lib/daqmx/configure/channels-llb/daqmx-configure-teds-vi.html) Associates TEDS information with the physical channel you specify. If you do not specify the filename of a data sheet in the virtual TEDS file input, this VI attempts to find a TEDS sensor connected to the physical channel. This VI temporarily overrides any TEDS configuration for the physical channel that you performed in MAX.
- [DAQmx Write TEDS Data VI](../../../../vi-lib/daqmx/configure/channels-llb/daqmx-write-teds-data-vi.html) Writes TEDS data to the TEDS sensor connected to the physical channel you specify. This VI can write TEDS data from a 1D array of 8-bit unsigned integers or from a virtual TEDS file.
- [DAQmx Clear TEDS VI](../../../../vi-lib/daqmx/configure/channels-llb/daqmx-clear-teds-vi.html) Removes TEDS information from the physical channel you specify. This VI temporarily overrides any TEDS configuration for the physical channel that you performed in MAX.
- [DAQmx Physical Channel Property Node](../../../../vi-lib/daqmx/configure/channels-llb/daqmx-physical-channel-property-node-vi.html) A Property Node with the DAQmx Physical Channel class preselected. Right-click the Property Node and choose Select Filter from the shortcut menu to make the Property Node show only the properties supported by a particular device installed in the system or supported by all the devices installed in the system.

Parent topic:

DAQmx Advanced

<!--NI_TOPIC bundle=ni-daqmx-labview-api-ref path=menus/categories/measurement/daqmx/timedloop-mnu.html language=enus -->
## TOPIC 00544: Timed Loop

- bundle_id: `ni-daqmx-labview-api-ref`
- source_path: `menus/categories/measurement/daqmx/timedloop-mnu.html`
- source_url: https://docs-be.ni.com/bundle/ni-daqmx-labview-api-ref/raw/resource/enus/menus/categories/measurement/daqmx/timedloop-mnu.html
- document_id: `ni-daqmx-labview-api-ref`
- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: `reference`
- source_description: Use the DAQmx Timed Loop VI and function to create and configure timing sources for Timed Loops. icon

### Timed Loop

Use the DAQmx Timed Loop VI and function to create and configure timing sources for Timed Loops.

[IMAGE alt='icon' src='timedloop-mnu.png']

- [DAQmx Create Timing Source VI](../../../../vi-lib/daqmx/create/timing-llb/daqmx-create-timing-source-vi.html) Creates a timing source for a Timed Loop. The timing source is based on signals a device generates. The instances of this polymorphic VI correspond to the type of signal to use for the timing source. Wire the timing source out output to the source input of the Input Node of a Timed Loop to use this timing source with that Timed Loop.
- [DAQmx Timing Source Property Node](../../../../vi-lib/daqmx/configure/timing-llb/daqmx-timing-source-property-node-vi.html) A Property Node with the DAQmx Timing Source class preselected. Right-click the Property Node and choose Select Filter from the shortcut menu to make the Property Node show only the properties supported by a particular device installed in the system or supported by all the devices installed in the system.

Parent topic:

DAQmx Real-Time

<!--NI_TOPIC bundle=ni-daqmx-labview-api-ref path=menus/categories/measurement/daqmx/watchdog-mnu.html language=enus -->
## TOPIC 00545: DAQmx Watchdog

- bundle_id: `ni-daqmx-labview-api-ref`
- source_path: `menus/categories/measurement/daqmx/watchdog-mnu.html`
- source_url: https://docs-be.ni.com/bundle/ni-daqmx-labview-api-ref/raw/resource/enus/menus/categories/measurement/daqmx/watchdog-mnu.html
- document_id: `ni-daqmx-labview-api-ref`
- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: `reference`
- source_description: Use the DAQmx Watchdog VIs and function to configure and control the watchdog timer of a device. icon

### DAQmx Watchdog

Use the DAQmx Watchdog VIs and function to configure and control the watchdog timer of a device.

[IMAGE alt='icon' src='watchdog-mnu.png']

- [DAQmx Create Watchdog Timer Task VI](../../../../vi-lib/daqmx/create/task-llb/daqmx-create-watchdog-timer-task-vi.html) Creates and configures a task that controls the watchdog timer of a device. The timer activates when you start the task. Use the digital physical channel expiration states input to set expiration states for digital channels. If your device supports expiration states for other channel types, use the DAQmx Configure Watchdog Expiration States to configure those channels' expiration states. This VI does not program the watchdog timer on a real-time controller. Use the Real-Time Watchdog VIs to program the watchdog timer on a real-time controller.
- [DAQmx Configure Watchdog Expiration States VI](../../../../vi-lib/daqmx/configure/task-llb/daqmx-configure-watchdog-expiration-states-vi.html) Configures the expiration states for a watchdog timer task.
- [DAQmx Control Watchdog Task VI](../../../../vi-lib/daqmx/configure/task-llb/daqmx-control-watchdog-task-vi.html) Controls the watchdog timer task according to the action you specify. This VI does not program the watchdog timer on a real-time controller. Use the Real-Time Watchdog VIs to program the watchdog timer on a real-time controller.
- [DAQmx Watchdog Property Node](../../../../vi-lib/daqmx/configure/task-llb/daqmx-watchdog-property-node-vi.html) A Property Node with the DAQmx Watchdog class preselected. Right-click the Property Node and choose Select Filter from the shortcut menu to make the Property Node show only the properties supported by a particular device installed in the system or supported by all devices installed in the system.

Parent topic:

DAQmx Device Configuration

<!--NI_TOPIC bundle=ni-daqmx-labview-api-ref path=resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-buffer-p.html language=enus -->
## TOPIC 00547: DAQmx Buffer Properties

- bundle_id: `ni-daqmx-labview-api-ref`
- source_path: `resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-buffer-p.html`
- source_url: https://docs-be.ni.com/bundle/ni-daqmx-labview-api-ref/raw/resource/enus/resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-buffer-p.html
- document_id: `ni-daqmx-labview-api-ref`
- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: `reference`
- source_description: Use the DAQmx Buffer properties to configure input and output buffers in computer memory and to query the size of device onboard buffers.

### DAQmx Buffer Properties

Use the DAQmx Buffer properties to configure input and output buffers in computer memory and to query the size of device onboard buffers.

- [Input:Buffer Size](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-buffer/attr186c.html) Specifies the number of samples the input buffer can hold for each channel in the task. Zero indicates to allocate no buffer. Use a buffer size of 0 to perform a hardware-timed operation without using a buffer. Setting this property overrides the automatic input buffer allocation that NI-DAQmx performs.
- [Input:Onboard Buffer Size](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-buffer/attr230a.html) Indicates in samples per channel the size of the onboard input buffer of the device.
- [Output:Buffer Size](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-buffer/attr186d.html) Specifies the number of samples the output buffer can hold for each channel in the task. Zero indicates to allocate no buffer. Use a buffer size of 0 to perform a hardware-timed operation without using a buffer. Setting this property overrides the automatic output buffer allocation that NI-DAQmx performs.
- [Output:Onboard Buffer Size](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-buffer/attr230b.html) Specifies in samples per channel the size of the onboard output buffer of the device.

<!--NI_TOPIC bundle=ni-daqmx-labview-api-ref path=resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-buffer/attr186c.html language=enus -->
## TOPIC 00548: Input:Buffer Size

- bundle_id: `ni-daqmx-labview-api-ref`
- source_path: `resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-buffer/attr186c.html`
- source_url: https://docs-be.ni.com/bundle/ni-daqmx-labview-api-ref/raw/resource/enus/resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-buffer/attr186c.html
- document_id: `ni-daqmx-labview-api-ref`
- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: `reference`
- source_description: Specifies the number of samples the input buffer can hold for each channel in the task. Zero indicates to allocate no buffer. Use a buffer size of 0 to perform a hardware-timed operation without using a buffer. Setting this property overrides the automatic input buffer allocation that NI-DAQmx perfo

### Input:Buffer Size

Specifies the number of samples the input buffer can hold for each channel in the task. Zero indicates to allocate no buffer. Use a buffer size of 0 to perform a hardware-timed operation without using a buffer. Setting this property overrides the 
 [automatic input buffer allocation](/csh?context=nidaqmx_mxcncpts_buffersize)
 that NI-DAQmx performs.

#### Remarks

The following table lists the [characteristics](/csh?productcategories=147794&context=lvcore_lvprop_flags) of this property.

| Short Name | Input.BufSize |
| --- | --- |
| Data type |  |
| Permissions | Read/Write |
| Resettable | True |
| Settable While Task Is Running | device-specific |
| Available in Run-Time Engine | True |

Parent topic:

DAQmx Buffer Properties

Use a buffer size of 0 to perform a hardware-timed operation without using a buffer. Setting this property overrides the automatic output buffer allocation that NI-DAQmx per

### Output:Buffer Size

Specifies the number of samples the output buffer can hold for each channel in the task. Zero indicates to allocate no buffer. Use a buffer size of 0 to perform a hardware-timed operation without using a buffer. Setting this property overrides the 
 [automatic output buffer allocation](/csh?context=nidaqmx_mxcncpts_buffersize)
 that NI-DAQmx performs.

| --- | --- |
| Data type |  |
| Permissions | Read/Write |
| Resettable | True |
| Settable While Task Is Running | device-specific |
| Available in Run-Time Engine | True |

<!--NI_TOPIC bundle=ni-daqmx-labview-api-ref path=resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-calibration-info-p.html language=enus -->
## TOPIC 00552: DAQmx Calibration Info Properties

- bundle_id: `ni-daqmx-labview-api-ref`
- source_path: `resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-calibration-info-p.html`
- source_url: https://docs-be.ni.com/bundle/ni-daqmx-labview-api-ref/raw/resource/enus/resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-calibration-info-p.html
- document_id: `ni-daqmx-labview-api-ref`
- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: `reference`
- source_description: The DAQmx Calibration Info properties return information about the calibration of a device.

### DAQmx Calibration Info Properties

The DAQmx Calibration Info properties return information about the calibration of a device.

- [Active Device](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-calibration-info/attr185f.html) Specifies the device from which to retrieve calibration properties.
- [External Calibration:Last External Calibration Date/Time](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-calibration-info/attr1865.html) Indicates the last date and time that the device underwent an external calibration.
- [External Calibration:Last External Calibration Temperature](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-calibration-info/attr1867.html) Indicates in degrees Celsius the temperature of the device at the time of the last external calibration. Compare this temperature to the current onboard temperature to determine if you should perform another calibration.
- [External Calibration:Recommended Interval](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-calibration-info/attr1868.html) Indicates in months the National Instruments recommended interval between each external calibration of the device.
- [More:Accessory Connection Count](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-calibration-info/attr2feb.html) Specifies the number of times a particular connection that results in tangible wear and tear of onboard components has been made on the accessory. This connection count is useful for tracking accessory life and usage.
- [More:Device Temperature](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-calibration-info/attr223b.html) Indicates in degrees Celsius the current temperature of the device.
- [More:Recommended Accessory Connection Count Limit](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-calibration-info/attr2fec.html) Indicates the recommended connection count limit for an accessory. If the accessory connection count exceeds this limit, the accessory could require maintenance.
- [Self Calibration:Is Supported](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-calibration-info/attr1860.html) Indicates whether the device supports self-calibration.
- [Self Calibration:Last Self Calibration Date/Time](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-calibration-info/attr1862.html) Indicates the last date and time that the device underwent a self-calibration.
- [Self Calibration:Last Self Calibration Temperature](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-calibration-info/attr1864.html) Indicates in degrees Celsius the temperature of the device at the time of the last self-calibration. Compare this temperature to the current onboard temperature to determine if you should perform another calibration.
- [User-Defined Information:Information](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-calibration-info/attr1861.html) Specifies a string that contains arbitrary, user-defined information. This number of characters in this string can be no more than Cal.UserDefinedInfo.MaxSize .
- [User-Defined Information:Max Size](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-calibration-info/attr191c.html) Indicates the maximum length in characters of Cal.UserDefinedInfo .

## TOPIC 00557: Self Calibration:Last Self Calibration Temperature

- bundle_id: `ni-daqmx-labview-api-ref`
- source_path: `resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-calibration-info/attr1864.html`
- source_url: https://docs-be.ni.com/bundle/ni-daqmx-labview-api-ref/raw/resource/enus/resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-calibration-info/attr1864.html
- document_id: `ni-daqmx-labview-api-ref`
- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: `reference`
- source_description: Indicates in degrees Celsius the temperature of the device at the time of the last self-calibration. Compare this temperature to the current onboard temperature to determine if you should perform another calibration. The temperature returned by this property is the calibration temperature as measure

### Self Calibration:Last Self Calibration Temperature

Indicates in degrees Celsius the temperature of the device at the time of the last self-calibration. Compare this temperature to the current onboard temperature to determine if you should perform another calibration.

The temperature returned by this property is the calibration temperature as measured by an onboard temperature sensor and may differ from the temperature displayed 
on a printed calibration certificate. Calibration certificates usually display the ambient temperature rather than the onboard 
temperature.

Using Traditional NI-DAQ (Legacy) to perform calibration does not update this property. This property is updated only when you use NI-DAQmx 
to perform calibration.

#### Remarks

The following table lists the [characteristics](/csh?productcategories=147794&context=lvcore_lvprop_flags) of this property.

| Short Name | SelfCal.LastTemp |
| --- | --- |
| Data type |  |
| Permissions | Read Only |
| Resettable | False |
| Settable While Task Is Running | device-specific |
| Available in Run-Time Engine | True |

Parent topic:

DAQmx Calibration Info Properties

<!--NI_TOPIC bundle=ni-daqmx-labview-api-ref path=resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-calibration-info/attr1865.html language=enus -->
