<!--NI_TOPIC bundle=ni-daqmx-labview-api-ref path=resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel-p.html language=enus -->
## TOPIC 00565: DAQmx Channel Properties

- bundle_id: `ni-daqmx-labview-api-ref`
- source_path: `resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel-p.html`
- source_url: https://docs-be.ni.com/bundle/ni-daqmx-labview-api-ref/raw/resource/enus/resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel-p.html
- document_id: `ni-daqmx-labview-api-ref`
- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: `reference`
- source_description: Use the DAQmx Channel properties to configure virtual channels.

### DAQmx Channel Properties

Use the DAQmx Channel properties to configure virtual channels.

- [Active Channels (if subset)](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr11.html) Specifies a virtual channel or list of virtual channels to modify. The virtual channels are within the context of a specific task . NI-DAQmx configures all channels in the task if you do not set this property.
- [Analog Input:Acceleration:4 Wire DC Voltage:Sensitivity](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr3115.html) Specifies the sensitivity of the 4 wire DC voltage acceleration sensor connected to the channel. This value is the units you specify with AI.Accel.4WireDCVoltage.SensitivityUnits. Refer to the sensor documentation to determine this value.
- [Analog Input:Acceleration:4 Wire DC Voltage:Sensitivity Units](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr3116.html) Specifies the units of AI.Accel.4WireDCVoltage.Sensitivity.
- [Analog Input:Acceleration:Accelerometer:Sensitivity](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr692.html) Specifies the sensitivity of the accelerometer . This value is in the units you specify with AI.Accel.SensitivityUnits . Refer to the sensor documentation to determine this value.
- [Analog Input:Acceleration:Accelerometer:Sensitivity Units](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr219c.html) Specifies the units of AI.Accel.Sensitivity .
- [Analog Input:Acceleration:Charge:Sensitivity](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr3113.html) Specifies the sensitivity of the charge acceleration sensor connected to the channel. This value is the units you specify with AI.Accel.Charge.SensitivityUnits. Refer to the sensor documentation to determine this value.
- [Analog Input:Acceleration:Charge:Sensitivity Units](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr3114.html) Specifies the units of AI.Accel.Charge.Sensitivity.
- [Analog Input:Acceleration:Units](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr673.html) Specifies the units to use to return acceleration measurements from the channel.
- [Analog Input:Acceleration:dB Reference](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr29b2.html) Specifies the decibel reference level in the units of the channel. When you read samples as a waveform, the decibel reference level is included in the waveform attributes.
- [Analog Input:Bridge:Scaling Parameters:Electrical Units](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr2f87.html) Specifies from which electrical unit to scale data. Select the same unit that the sensor data sheet or calibration certificate uses for electrical values.
- [Analog Input:Bridge:Scaling Parameters:Physical Units](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr2f88.html) Specifies to which physical unit to scale electrical data. Select the same unit that the sensor data sheet or calibration certificate uses for physical values.
- [Analog Input:Bridge:Scaling Parameters:Polynomial:Forward Coefficients](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr2f90.html) Specifies an array of coefficients for the polynomial that converts electrical values to physical values. Each element of the array corresponds to a term of the equation. For example, if index three of the array is 9, the fourth term of the equation is 9x^3.
- [Analog Input:Bridge:Scaling Parameters:Polynomial:Reverse Coefficients](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr2f91.html) Specifies an array of coefficients for the polynomial that converts physical values to electrical values. Each element of the array corresponds to a term of the equation. For example, if index three of the array is 9, the fourth term of the equation is 9x^3.
- [Analog Input:Bridge:Scaling Parameters:Scale Type](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr2f89.html) Specifies the scaling type to use when scaling electrical values from the sensor to physical units.
- [Analog Input:Bridge:Scaling Parameters:Table:Electrical Values](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr2f8e.html) Specifies the array of electrical values that map to the values in AI.Bridge.Table.PhysicalVals . Specify this value in the unit indicated by AI.Bridge.ElectricalUnits .
- [Analog Input:Bridge:Scaling Parameters:Table:Physical Values](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr2f8f.html) Specifies the array of physical values that map to the values in AI.Bridge.Table.ElectricalVals . Specify this value in the unit indicated by AI.Bridge.PhysicalUnits .
- [Analog Input:Bridge:Scaling Parameters:Two-Point Linear:First:Electrical Value](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr2f8a.html) Specifies the first electrical value, corresponding to AI.Bridge.TwoPointLin.First.PhysicalVal . Specify this value in the unit indicated by AI.Bridge.ElectricalUnits .
- [Analog Input:Bridge:Scaling Parameters:Two-Point Linear:First:Physical Value](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr2f8b.html) Specifies the first physical value, corresponding to AI.Bridge.TwoPointLin.First.ElectricalVal . Specify this value in the unit indicated by AI.Bridge.PhysicalUnits .
- [Analog Input:Bridge:Scaling Parameters:Two-Point Linear:Second:Electrical Value](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr2f8c.html) Specifies the second electrical value, corresponding to AI.Bridge.TwoPointLin.Second.PhysicalVal . Specify this value in the unit indicated by AI.Bridge.ElectricalUnits .
- [Analog Input:Bridge:Scaling Parameters:Two-Point Linear:Second:Physical Value](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr2f8d.html) Specifies the second physical value, corresponding to AI.Bridge.TwoPointLin.Second.ElectricalVal . Specify this value in the unit indicated by AI.Bridge.PhysicalUnits .
- [Analog Input:Bridge:Units](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr2f92.html) Specifies in which unit to return voltage ratios from the channel.
- [Analog Input:Calculated Power:Current Maximum Value](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr31ef.html) Specifies the current maximum value you expect to measure. This value is in the units you specify with a units property. When you query this property, it returns the coerced current maximum value that the device can measure with the current settings.
- [Analog Input:Calculated Power:Current Minimum Value](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr31f0.html) Specifies the current minimum value you expect to measure. This value is in the units you specify with a units property. When you query this property, it returns the coerced current minimum value that the device can measure with the current settings.
- [Analog Input:Calculated Power:Units](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr31ec.html) Specifies the units to use to return power measurements from the channel.
- [Analog Input:Calculated Power:Voltage Maximum Value](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr31ed.html) Specifies the voltage maximum value you expect to measure. This value is in the units you specify with a units property. When you query this property, it returns the coerced voltage maximum value that the device can measure with the current settings.
- [Analog Input:Calculated Power:Voltage Minimum Value](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr31ee.html) Specifies the voltage minimum value you expect to measure. This value is in the units you specify with a units property. When you query this property, it returns the coerced voltage minimum value that the device can measure with the current settings.
- [Analog Input:Charge:Units](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr3112.html) Specifies the units to use to return charge measurements from the channel.
- [Analog Input:Current:AC RMS Current:Units](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr17e3.html) Specifies the units to use to return current RMS measurements from the channel.
- [Analog Input:Current:Units](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr701.html) Specifies the units to use to return current measurements from the channel.
- [Analog Input:Custom Scale Name](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr17e0.html) Specifies the name of a custom scale for the channel.
- [Analog Input:Force:IEPE Sensor:Sensitivity](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr2f81.html) Specifies the sensitivity of the IEPE force sensor connected to the channel. Specify this value in the unit indicated by AI.Force.IEPESensor.SensitivityUnits .
- [Analog Input:Force:IEPE Sensor:Sensitivity Units](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr2f82.html) Specifies the units for AI.Force.IEPESensor.Sensitivity .
- [Analog Input:Force:Units](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr2f75.html) Specifies in which unit to return force or load measurements from the channel.
- [Analog Input:Frequency:Units](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr806.html) Specifies the units to use to return frequency measurements from the channel.
- [Analog Input:Frequency:Voltage:Hysteresis](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr814.html) Specifies in volts a window below AI.Freq.ThreshVoltage . The input voltage must pass below AI.Freq.ThreshVoltage minus this value before NI-DAQmx recognizes a waveform repetition at AI.Freq.ThreshVoltage . Hysteresis can improve the measurement accuracy when the signal contains noise or jitter.
- [Analog Input:Frequency:Voltage:Threshold Level](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr815.html) Specifies the voltage level at which to recognize waveform repetitions. You should select a voltage level that occurs only once within the entire period of a waveform. You also can select a voltage that occurs only once while the voltage rises or falls.
- [Analog Input:General Properties:Advanced:DC Offset](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr2a89.html) Specifies the DC value to add to the input range of the device. Use AI.Rng.High and AI.Rng.Low to specify the input range. This offset is in the native units of the device .
- [Analog Input:General Properties:Advanced:Data Transfer and Memory:Compression:Lossy LSB Removal:Compressed Sample Size](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr22d9.html) Specifies the number of bits to return in a raw sample when AI.RawDataCompressionType is set to Lossy LSB Removal.
- [Analog Input:General Properties:Advanced:Data Transfer and Memory:Compression:Raw Data Compression Type](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr22d8.html) Specifies the type of compression to apply to raw samples returned from the device.
- [Analog Input:General Properties:Advanced:Data Transfer and Memory:Data Transfer Custom Threshold](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr230c.html) Specifies the number of samples that must be in the FIFO to transfer data from the device if AI.DataXferReqCond is Onboard Memory Custom Threshold.
- [Analog Input:General Properties:Advanced:Data Transfer and Memory:Data Transfer Maximum Rate](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr3117.html) Specifies the rate in B/s to transfer data from the device. If this value is not set, then the device will transfer data at a rate based on the bus detected. Modify this value to affect performance under different combinations of operating system, configuration, and device.
- [Analog Input:General Properties:Advanced:Data Transfer and Memory:Data Transfer Mechanism](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr1821.html) Specifies the data transfer mode for the device.
- [Analog Input:General Properties:Advanced:Data Transfer and Memory:Data Transfer Request Condition](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr188b.html) Specifies under what condition to transfer data from the onboard memory of the device to the buffer.
- [Analog Input:General Properties:Advanced:Data Transfer and Memory:Memory Mapping for Programmed IO Enable](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr188c.html) Specifies for NI-DAQmx to map hardware registers to the memory space of the application, if possible. Normally, NI-DAQmx maps hardware registers to memory accessible only to the kernel. Mapping the registers to the memory space of the application increases performance. However, if the application accesses the memory space mapped to the registers, it can adversely affect the operation of the device and possibly result in a system crash.
- [Analog Input:General Properties:Advanced:Data Transfer and Memory:USB Transfer Request Count](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr3000.html) Specifies the maximum number of simultaneous USB transfers used to stream data. Modify this value to affect performance under different combinations of operating system and device.
- [Analog Input:General Properties:Advanced:Data Transfer and Memory:USB Transfer Request Size](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr2a8e.html) Specifies the maximum size of a USB transfer request in bytes. Modify this value to affect performance under different combinations of operating system and device.
- [Analog Input:General Properties:Advanced:Device Scaling Coefficients:Device Scaling Coefficients](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr1930.html) Indicates the coefficients of a polynomial equation that NI-DAQmx uses to scale values from the native format of the device to volts. Each element of the array corresponds to a term of the equation. For example, if index two of the array is 4, the third term of the equation is 4x^2. Scaling coefficients do not account for any custom scales or sensors contained by the channel.
- [Analog Input:General Properties:Advanced:Enhanced Alias Rejection Enable](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr2294.html) Specifies whether to enable enhanced alias rejection . Leave this property set to the default value for most applications.
- [Analog Input:General Properties:Advanced:Gain](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr1818.html) Specifies a gain factor to apply to the channel.
- [Analog Input:General Properties:Advanced:High Accuracy Settings:Auto Zero Mode](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr1760.html) Specifies how often to measure ground. NI-DAQmx subtracts the measured ground voltage from every sample.
- [Analog Input:General Properties:Advanced:High Accuracy Settings:Chop:Enable](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr3143.html) Specifies whether the device will chop its inputs. Chopping removes offset voltages and other low frequency errors.
- [Analog Input:General Properties:Advanced:Input Limits Fault Detection:Enable](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr318e.html) Specifies whether to enable input limits fault detection.
- [Analog Input:General Properties:Advanced:Input Limits Fault Detection:Lower Limit](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr318d.html) Specifies the level of the lower limit for input limits detection. An input sample outside the upper and lower bounds causes a fault. Note: Fault detection applies to both positive and negative inputs. For instance, if you specify a lower limit of 2 mA and an upper limit of 12 mA, NI-DAQmx detects a fault at 15 mA and -15 mA, but not at -6 mA because it is in the range of -12 mA to -2 mA.
- [Analog Input:General Properties:Advanced:Input Limits Fault Detection:Upper Limit](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr318c.html) Specifies the level of the upper limit for input limits detection. An input sample outside the upper and lower bounds causes a fault. Note: Fault detection applies to both positive and negative inputs. For instance, if you specify a lower limit of 2 mA and an upper limit of 12 mA, NI-DAQmx detects a fault at 15 mA and -15 mA, but not at -6 mA because it is in the range of -12 mA to -2 mA.
- [Analog Input:General Properties:Advanced:Open Channel Detection Enable](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr30ff.html) Specifies whether to enable open channel detection.
- [Analog Input:General Properties:Advanced:Overcurrent Detection:Enable](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr3194.html) Specifies whether to enable overcurrent detection.
- [Analog Input:General Properties:Advanced:Power Supply Fault Detection:Enable](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr3191.html) Specifies whether to enable power supply fault detection.
- [Analog Input:General Properties:Advanced:Range:High](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr1815.html) Specifies the upper limit of the input range of the device. This value is in the native units of the device. On E Series devices, for example, the native units is volts.
- [Analog Input:General Properties:Advanced:Range:Low](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr1816.html) Specifies the lower limit of the input range of the device. This value is in the native units of the device. On E Series devices, for example, the native units is volts.
- [Analog Input:General Properties:Advanced:Sample and Hold Enable](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr181a.html) Specifies whether to enable the sample and hold circuitry of the device. When you disable sample and hold circuitry, a small voltage offset might be introduced into the signal. You can eliminate this offset by using AI.AutoZeroMode to perform an auto zero on the channel.
- [Analog Input:General Properties:Channel Calibration:Apply Calibration If Expired](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr2299.html) Specifies whether to apply the channel calibration to the channel after the expiration date has passed.
- [Analog Input:General Properties:Channel Calibration:Calibration Date](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr229a.html) Specifies the last date and time that the channel underwent a channel calibration.
- [Analog Input:General Properties:Channel Calibration:Description](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr22a4.html) Specifies the description entered for the calibration of the channel.
- [Analog Input:General Properties:Channel Calibration:Enable Calibration](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr2298.html) Specifies whether to enable the channel calibration associated with the channel.
- [Analog Input:General Properties:Channel Calibration:Expiration Date](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr229b.html) Specifies the date and time that the channel calibration expires.
- [Analog Input:General Properties:Channel Calibration:Has Valid Calibration Information](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr2297.html) Indicates if the channel has calibration information.
- [Analog Input:General Properties:Channel Calibration:Operator Name](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr22a3.html) Specifies the name of the operator who performed the channel calibration.
- [Analog Input:General Properties:Channel Calibration:Scaling Parameters:Polynomial:Forward Coefficients](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr229f.html) Specifies the forward polynomial values used for calibrating the channel.
- [Analog Input:General Properties:Channel Calibration:Scaling Parameters:Polynomial:Reverse Coefficients](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr22a0.html) Specifies the reverse polynomial values used for calibrating the channel.
- [Analog Input:General Properties:Channel Calibration:Scaling Parameters:Scale Type](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr229c.html) Specifies the method or equation form that the calibration scale uses.
- [Analog Input:General Properties:Channel Calibration:Scaling Parameters:Table:Pre-Scaled Values](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr229d.html) Specifies the reference values collected when calibrating the channel.
- [Analog Input:General Properties:Channel Calibration:Scaling Parameters:Table:Scaled Values](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr229e.html) Specifies the acquired values collected when calibrating the channel.
- [Analog Input:General Properties:Channel Calibration:Verification:Acquired Values](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr22a2.html) Specifies the acquired values collected when verifying the calibration. NI-DAQmx stores these values as a record of calibration accuracy and does not use them in the scaling process.
- [Analog Input:General Properties:Channel Calibration:Verification:Reference Values](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr22a1.html) Specifies the reference values collected when verifying the calibration. NI-DAQmx stores these values as a record of calibration accuracy and does not use them in the scaling process.
- [Analog Input:General Properties:Digitizer/ADC:Custom Timing Mode](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr2f6b.html) Specifies the timing mode of the ADC when AI.ADCTimingMode is Custom.
- [Analog Input:General Properties:Digitizer/ADC:Dither:Enable](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr68.html) Specifies whether to enable dithering. Dithering adds Gaussian noise to the input signal. You can use dithering to achieve higher resolution measurements by over sampling the input signal and averaging the results.
- [Analog Input:General Properties:Digitizer/ADC:Raw Sample Justification](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr50.html) Indicates the justification of a raw sample from the device.
- [Analog Input:General Properties:Digitizer/ADC:Raw Sample Size](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr22da.html) Indicates in bits the size of a raw sample from the device.
- [Analog Input:General Properties:Digitizer/ADC:Resolution Units](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr1764.html) Indicates the units of AI.Resolution .
- [Analog Input:General Properties:Digitizer/ADC:Resolution Value](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr1765.html) Indicates the resolution of the analog-to-digital converter of the channel. This value is in the units you specify with AI.ResolutionUnits .
- [Analog Input:General Properties:Digitizer/ADC:Timing Mode](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr29f9.html) Specifies the ADC timing mode , controlling the tradeoff between speed and effective resolution. Some ADC timing modes provide increased powerline noise rejection. On devices that have an AI Convert clock, this setting affects both the maximum and default values for AIConv.Rate . You must use the same ADC timing mode for all channels on a device, but you can use different ADC timing modes for different devices in the same task.
- [Analog Input:General Properties:Filter:Analog Filter:Lowpass:Advanced:Switched Capacitor:Clock Source](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr1884.html) Specifies the source of the filter clock. If you need a higher resolution for the filter, you can supply an external clock to increase the resolution. Refer to the SCXI-1141/1142/1143 User Manual for more information.
- [Analog Input:General Properties:Filter:Analog Filter:Lowpass:Advanced:Switched Capacitor:External Clock Divisor](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr1886.html) Specifies the divisor for the external clock when you set AI.Lowpass.SwitchCap.ClkSrc to External. On the SCXI-1141, SCXI-1142, and SCXI-1143, NI-DAQmx determines the filter cutoff by using the equation f/(100*n), where f is the external frequency, and n is the external clock divisor. Refer to the SCXI-1141/1142/1143 User Manual for more information.
- [Analog Input:General Properties:Filter:Analog Filter:Lowpass:Advanced:Switched Capacitor:External Clock Frequency](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr1885.html) Specifies the frequency of the external clock when you set AI.Lowpass.SwitchCap.ClkSrc to External. NI-DAQmx uses this frequency to set the pre- and post- filters on the SCXI-1141, SCXI-1142, and SCXI-1143. On those devices, NI-DAQmx determines the filter cutoff by using the equation f/(100*n), where f is the external frequency, and n is the external clock divisor. Refer to the SCXI-1141/1142/1143 User Manual for more information.
- [Analog Input:General Properties:Filter:Analog Filter:Lowpass:Advanced:Switched Capacitor:Output Clock Divisor](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr1887.html) Specifies the divisor for the output clock. NI-DAQmx uses the cutoff frequency to determine the output clock frequency. Refer to the SCXI-1141/1142/1143 User Manual for more information.
- [Analog Input:General Properties:Filter:Analog Filter:Lowpass:Cutoff Frequency](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr1803.html) Specifies the frequency in Hertz that corresponds to the -3dB cutoff of the filter.
- [Analog Input:General Properties:Filter:Analog Filter:Lowpass:Enable](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr1802.html) Specifies whether to enable the lowpass filter of the channel.
- [Analog Input:General Properties:Filter:Averaging Window Size](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr2fee.html) Specifies the number of samples to average while acquiring data. Increasing the number of samples to average reduces noise in your measurement.
- [Analog Input:General Properties:Filter:Digital Filter:Advanced:Coefficients](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr30c7.html) Specifies the digital filter coefficients.
- [Analog Input:General Properties:Filter:Digital Filter:Bandpass:Center Frequency](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr30c3.html) Specifies the center frequency of the passband for the digital filter.
- [Analog Input:General Properties:Filter:Digital Filter:Bandpass:Width](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr30c4.html) Specifies the width of the passband centered around the center frequency for the digital filter.
- [Analog Input:General Properties:Filter:Digital Filter:Enable](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr30bd.html) Specifies whether the digital filter is enabled or disabled.
- [Analog Input:General Properties:Filter:Digital Filter:Highpass:Cutoff Frequency](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr30c2.html) Specifies the highpass cutoff frequency of the digital filter.
- [Analog Input:General Properties:Filter:Digital Filter:Lowpass:Cutoff Frequency](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr30c1.html) Specifies the lowpass cutoff frequency of the digital filter.
- [Analog Input:General Properties:Filter:Digital Filter:Notch:Center Frequency](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr30c5.html) Specifies the center frequency of the stopband for the digital filter.
- [Analog Input:General Properties:Filter:Digital Filter:Notch:Width](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr30c6.html) Specifies the width of the stopband centered around the center frequency for the digital filter.
- [Analog Input:General Properties:Filter:Digital Filter:Order](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr30c0.html) Specifies the order of the digital filter.
- [Analog Input:General Properties:Filter:Digital Filter:Response](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr30bf.html) Specifies the digital filter response.
- [Analog Input:General Properties:Filter:Digital Filter:Type](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr30be.html) Specifies the digital filter type.
- [Analog Input:General Properties:Filter:Enable](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr3173.html) Specifies the corresponding filter enable/disable state.
- [Analog Input:General Properties:Filter:Filter Delay](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr2fed.html) Indicates the amount of time between when the ADC samples data and when the sample is read by the host device. This value is in the units you specify with AI.FilterDelayUnits . You can adjust this amount of time using AI.FilterDelayAdjustment .
- [Analog Input:General Properties:Filter:Filter Delay Adjustment](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr3074.html) Specifies the amount of filter delay that gets removed if AI.RemoveFilterDelay is enabled. This delay adjustment is in addition to the value indicated by AI.FilterDelay . This delay adjustment is in the units you specify with AI.FilterDelayUnits .
- [Analog Input:General Properties:Filter:Filter Delay Units](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr3071.html) Specifies the units of AI.FilterDelay and AI.FilterDelayAdjustment .
- [Analog Input:General Properties:Filter:Frequency](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr3174.html) Specifies the corresponding filter frequency (cutoff or center) of the filter response.
- [Analog Input:General Properties:Filter:Order](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr3176.html) Specifies the corresponding filter order and defines the slope of the filter response.
- [Analog Input:General Properties:Filter:Remove Filter Delay](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr2fbd.html) Specifies if filter delay removal is enabled on the device.
- [Analog Input:General Properties:Filter:Response](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr3175.html) Specifies the corresponding filter response and defines the shape of the filter response.
- [Analog Input:General Properties:Input Configuration:Coupling](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr64.html) Specifies the coupling for the channel.
- [Analog Input:General Properties:Input Configuration:Impedance](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr62.html) Specifies the input impedance of the channel.
- [Analog Input:General Properties:Input Configuration:Input Source](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr2198.html) Specifies the source of the channel. You can use the signal from the I/O connector or one of several calibration signals. Certain devices have a single calibration signal bus. For these devices, you must specify the same calibration signal for all channels you connect to a calibration signal.
- [Analog Input:General Properties:Input Configuration:Terminal Configuration](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr1097.html) Specifies the terminal configuration for the channel.
- [Analog Input:General Properties:Signal Conditioning:Attenuation](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr1801.html) Specifies the amount of attenuation to use.
- [Analog Input:General Properties:Signal Conditioning:Bridge:Balance:Coarse Potentiometer](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr17f1.html) Specifies by how much to compensate for offset in the signal. This value can be between 0 and 127.
- [Analog Input:General Properties:Signal Conditioning:Bridge:Balance:Fine Potentiometer](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr18f4.html) Specifies by how much to compensate for offset in the signal. This value can be between 0 and 4095.
- [Analog Input:General Properties:Signal Conditioning:Bridge:Configuration](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr87.html) Specifies the type of Wheatstone bridge connected to the channel.
- [Analog Input:General Properties:Signal Conditioning:Bridge:Initial Bridge Ratio](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr2f86.html) Specifies in volts per volt the ratio of output voltage from the bridge to excitation voltage supplied to the bridge while not under load. NI-DAQmx subtracts this value from any measurements before applying scaling equations. If you set AI.Bridge.InitialVoltage , NI-DAQmx coerces this property to AI.Bridge.InitialVoltage divided by AI.Excit.ActualVal . If you set this property, NI-DAQmx coerces AI.Bridge.InitialVoltage to the value of this property times AI.Excit.ActualVal . If you set both this property and AI.Bridge.InitialVoltage , and their values conflict, NI-DAQmx returns an error. To avoid this error, reset one property to its default value before setting the other.
- [Analog Input:General Properties:Signal Conditioning:Bridge:Initial Bridge Voltage](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr17ed.html) Specifies in volts the output voltage of the bridge while not under load. NI-DAQmx subtracts this value from any measurements before applying scaling equations. If you set AI.Bridge.InitialRatio , NI-DAQmx coerces this property to AI.Bridge.InitialRatio times AI.Excit.ActualVal . This property is set by DAQmx Perform Bridge Offset Nulling Calibration. If you set this property, NI-DAQmx coerces AI.Bridge.InitialRatio to the value of this property divided by AI.Excit.ActualVal . If you set both this property and AI.Bridge.InitialRatio , and their values conflict, NI-DAQmx returns an error. To avoid this error, reset one property to its default value before setting the other.
- [Analog Input:General Properties:Signal Conditioning:Bridge:Nominal Resistance](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr17ec.html) Specifies in ohms the resistance of the bridge while not under load.
- [Analog Input:General Properties:Signal Conditioning:Bridge:Shunt Cal:Gain Adjustment](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr193f.html) Specifies the result of a shunt calibration. This property is set by DAQmx Perform Shunt Calibration. NI-DAQmx multiplies data read from the channel by the value of this property. This value should be close to 1.0.
- [Analog Input:General Properties:Signal Conditioning:Bridge:Shunt Cal:Shunt Cal A Actual Resistor Value](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr2f79.html) Specifies in ohms the actual value of the internal shunt calibration A resistor.
- [Analog Input:General Properties:Signal Conditioning:Bridge:Shunt Cal:Shunt Cal A Resistor Value](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr2f78.html) Specifies in ohms the desired value of the internal shunt calibration A resistor.
- [Analog Input:General Properties:Signal Conditioning:Bridge:Shunt Cal:Shunt Cal A Source](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr30ca.html) Specifies whether to use internal or external shunt when Shunt Cal A is selected.
- [Analog Input:General Properties:Signal Conditioning:Bridge:Shunt Cal:Shunt Cal B Actual Resistor Value](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr2f7b.html) Specifies in ohms the actual value of the internal shunt calibration B resistor.
- [Analog Input:General Properties:Signal Conditioning:Bridge:Shunt Cal:Shunt Cal B Resistor Value](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr2f7a.html) Specifies in ohms the desired value of the internal shunt calibration B resistor.
- [Analog Input:General Properties:Signal Conditioning:Bridge:Shunt Cal:Shunt Cal Enable](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr94.html) Specifies whether to enable a shunt calibration switch. Use AI.Bridge.ShuntCal.Select to select the switch(es) to enable.
- [Analog Input:General Properties:Signal Conditioning:Bridge:Shunt Cal:Shunt Cal Select](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr21d5.html) Specifies which shunt calibration switch(es) to enable. Use AI.Bridge.ShuntCal.Enable to enable the switch(es) you specify with this property.
- [Analog Input:General Properties:Signal Conditioning:Current Shunt Resistor:Location](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr17f2.html) Specifies the shunt resistor location for current measurements.
- [Analog Input:General Properties:Signal Conditioning:Current Shunt Resistor:Value](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr17f3.html) Specifies in ohms the external shunt resistance for current measurements.
- [Analog Input:General Properties:Signal Conditioning:Excitation:AC Excitation:Frequency](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr101.html) Specifies the AC excitation frequency in Hertz.
- [Analog Input:General Properties:Signal Conditioning:Excitation:AC Excitation:Synchronization Enable](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr102.html) Specifies whether to synchronize the AC excitation source of the channel to that of another channel. Synchronize the excitation sources of multiple channels to use multichannel sensors. Set this property to FALSE for the master channel and to TRUE for the slave channels.
- [Analog Input:General Properties:Signal Conditioning:Excitation:AC Excitation:Wire Mode](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr18cd.html) Specifies the number of leads on the LVDT or RVDT. Some sensors require you to tie leads together to create a four- or five- wire sensor. Refer to the sensor documentation for more information.
- [Analog Input:General Properties:Signal Conditioning:Excitation:Advanced:Actual Excitation Value](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr1883.html) Specifies the actual amount of excitation supplied by an internal excitation source. If you read an internal excitation source more precisely with an external device, set this property to the value you read. NI-DAQmx ignores this value for external excitation. When performing shunt calibration, some devices set this property automatically.
- [Analog Input:General Properties:Signal Conditioning:Excitation:Advanced:DC or AC](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr17fb.html) Specifies if the excitation supply is DC or AC.
- [Analog Input:General Properties:Signal Conditioning:Excitation:Advanced:Idle Output Behavior](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr30b8.html) Specifies whether this channel will disable excitation after the task is uncommitted. Setting this to Zero Volts or Amps disables excitation after task uncommit. Setting this attribute to Maintain Existing Value leaves the excitation on after task uncommit.
- [Analog Input:General Properties:Signal Conditioning:Excitation:Advanced:Use Excitation For Scaling](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr17fc.html) Specifies if NI-DAQmx divides the measurement by the excitation. You should typically set this property to TRUE for ratiometric transducers. If you set this property to TRUE, set AI.Max and AI.Min to reflect the scaling.
- [Analog Input:General Properties:Signal Conditioning:Excitation:Advanced:Use Multiplexed Excitation](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr2180.html) Specifies if the SCXI-1122 multiplexes the excitation to the upper half of the channels as it advances through the scan list.
- [Analog Input:General Properties:Signal Conditioning:Excitation:Advanced:Voltage or Current](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr17f6.html) Specifies if the channel uses current or voltage excitation.
- [Analog Input:General Properties:Signal Conditioning:Excitation:Sense](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr30fd.html) Specifies whether to use local or remote sense to sense excitation.
- [Analog Input:General Properties:Signal Conditioning:Excitation:Source](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr17f4.html) Specifies the source of excitation.
- [Analog Input:General Properties:Signal Conditioning:Excitation:Value](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr17f5.html) Specifies the amount of excitation that the sensor requires. If AI.Excit.VoltageOrCurrent is Voltage, this value is in volts. If AI.Excit.VoltageOrCurrent is Current, this value is in amperes.
- [Analog Input:General Properties:Signal Conditioning:Lead Wire Resistance](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr17ee.html) Specifies in ohms the resistance of the wires that lead to the sensor.
- [Analog Input:General Properties:Signal Conditioning:Probe Attenuation](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr2a88.html) Specifies the amount of attenuation provided by the probe connected to the channel. Specify this attenuation as a ratio.
- [Analog Input:General Properties:Signal Conditioning:Resistance Configuration](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr1881.html) Specifies the resistance configuration for the channel. NI-DAQmx uses this value for any resistance-based measurements, including temperature measurement using a thermistor or RTD.
- [Analog Input:General Properties:Signal Conditioning:Sensor Power:Configuration](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr316a.html) Specifies whether to turn on the sensor's power supply or to leave the configuration unchanged.
- [Analog Input:General Properties:Signal Conditioning:Sensor Power:Type](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr316b.html) Specifies the type of power supplied to the sensor.
- [Analog Input:General Properties:Signal Conditioning:Sensor Power:Voltage](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr3169.html) Specifies the voltage level for the sensor's power supply.
- [Analog Input:General Properties:Signal Conditioning:Thermocouple:Lead Offset Voltage](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr2fb8.html) Specifies the lead offset nulling voltage to subtract from measurements on a device. This property is ignored if open thermocouple detection is disabled.
- [Analog Input:General Properties:Signal Conditioning:Thermocouple:Open Thermocouple Detection Enable](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr2f72.html) Specifies whether to apply the open thermocouple detection bias voltage to the channel. Changing the value of this property on a channel may require settling time before the data returned is valid. To compensate for this settling time, discard unsettled data or add a delay between committing and starting the task. Refer to your device specifications for the required settling time. When open thermocouple detection is enabled, use OpenThrmcplChansExist to determine if any channels were open.
- [Analog Input:Maximum Value](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr17dd.html) Specifies the maximum value you expect to measure. This value is in the units you specify with a units property. When you query this property, it returns the coerced maximum value that the device can measure with the current settings.
- [Analog Input:Measurement Type](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr695.html) Indicates the measurement to take with the analog input channel and in some cases, such as for temperature measurements, the sensor to use.
- [Analog Input:Minimum Value](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr17de.html) Specifies the minimum value you expect to measure. This value is in the units you specify with a units property. When you query this property, it returns the coerced minimum value that the device can measure with the current settings.
- [Analog Input:Position:Eddy Current Proximity Probe:Sensitivity](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr2abe.html) Specifies the sensitivity of the eddy current proximity probe . This value is in the units you specify with AI.EddyCurrentProx.SensitivityUnits . Refer to the sensor documentation to determine this value.
- [Analog Input:Position:Eddy Current Proximity Probe:Sensitivity Units](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr2abf.html) Specifies the units of AI.EddyCurrentProx.Sensitivity .
- [Analog Input:Position:Eddy Current Proximity Probe:Units](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr2ac0.html) Specifies the units to use to return proximity measurements from the channel.
- [Analog Input:Position:LVDT:Sensitivity](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr939.html) Specifies the sensitivity of the LVDT . This value is in the units you specify with AI.LVDT.SensitivityUnits . Refer to the sensor documentation to determine this value.
- [Analog Input:Position:LVDT:Sensitivity Units](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr219a.html) Specifies the units of AI.LVDT.Sensitivity .
- [Analog Input:Position:LVDT:Units](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr910.html) Specifies the units to use to return linear position measurements from the channel.
- [Analog Input:Position:RVDT:Sensitivity](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr903.html) Specifies the sensitivity of the RVDT . This value is in the units you specify with AI.RVDT.SensitivityUnits . Refer to the sensor documentation to determine this value.
- [Analog Input:Position:RVDT:Sensitivity Units](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr219b.html) Specifies the units of AI.RVDT.Sensitivity .
- [Analog Input:Position:RVDT:Units](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr877.html) Specifies the units to use to return angular position measurements from the channel.
- [Analog Input:Pressure:Units](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr2f76.html) Specifies in which unit to return pressure measurements from the channel.
- [Analog Input:Resistance:Units](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr955.html) Specifies the units to use to return resistance measurements.
- [Analog Input:Rosette Strain Gage:Gage Orientation](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr2ffc.html) Specifies gage orientation in degrees with respect to the X axis.
- [Analog Input:Rosette Strain Gage:Rosette Measurement Type](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr2ffd.html) Specifies the type of rosette measurement.
- [Analog Input:Rosette Strain Gage:Rosette Type](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr2ffe.html) Indicates the type of rosette gage.
- [Analog Input:Rosette Strain Gage:Strain Channels](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr2ffb.html) Indicates the raw strain channels that comprise the strain rosette.
- [Analog Input:Sound Pressure:Maximum Sound Pressure Level](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr223a.html) Specifies the maximum instantaneous sound pressure level you expect to measure. This value is in decibels, referenced to 20 micropascals. NI-DAQmx uses the maximum sound pressure level to calculate values in pascals for AI.Max and AI.Min for the channel.
- [Analog Input:Sound Pressure:Microphone:Sensitivity](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr1536.html) Specifies the sensitivity of the microphone . This value is in mV/Pa. Refer to the sensor documentation to determine this value.
- [Analog Input:Sound Pressure:Units](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr1528.html) Specifies the units to use to return sound pressure measurements from the channel.
- [Analog Input:Sound Pressure:dB Reference](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr29b1.html) Specifies the decibel reference level in the units of the channel. When you read samples as a waveform, the decibel reference level is included in the waveform attributes. NI-DAQmx also uses the decibel reference level when converting AI.SoundPressure.MaxSoundPressureLvl to a voltage level.
- [Analog Input:Strain:Force Read From Channel](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr2ffa.html) Specifies whether the data is returned by DAQmx Read when set on a raw strain channel that is part of a rosette configuration.
- [Analog Input:Strain:Strain Gage:Configuration](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr982.html) Specifies the bridge configuration of the strain gages.
- [Analog Input:Strain:Strain Gage:Gage Factor](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr994.html) Specifies the sensitivity of the strain gage. Gage factor relates the change in electrical resistance to the change in strain. Refer to the sensor documentation for this value.
- [Analog Input:Strain:Strain Gage:Poisson Ratio](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr998.html) Specifies the ratio of lateral strain to axial strain in the material you are measuring.
- [Analog Input:Strain:Units](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr981.html) Specifies the units to use to return strain measurements from the channel.
- [Analog Input:TEDS:Is TEDS](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr2983.html) Indicates if the virtual channel was initialized using a TEDS bitstream from the corresponding physical channel.
- [Analog Input:TEDS:Units](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr21e0.html) Indicates the units defined by TEDS information associated with the channel.
- [Analog Input:Temperature:Advanced:Force Read From Channel](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr18f8.html) Specifies whether to read from the channel if it is a cold-junction compensation channel. By default, DAQmx Read does not return data from cold-junction compensation channels. Setting this property to TRUE forces read operations to return the cold-junction compensation channel data with the other channels in the task.
- [Analog Input:Temperature:RTD:Custom:A](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr1010.html) Specifies the 'A' constant of the Callendar-Van Dusen equation . NI-DAQmx requires this value when you use a custom RTD.
- [Analog Input:Temperature:RTD:Custom:B](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr1011.html) Specifies the 'B' constant of the Callendar-Van Dusen equation . NI-DAQmx requires this value when you use a custom RTD.
- [Analog Input:Temperature:RTD:Custom:C](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr1013.html) Specifies the 'C' constant of the Callendar-Van Dusen equation . NI-DAQmx requires this value when you use a custom RTD.
- [Analog Input:Temperature:RTD:R0](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr1030.html) Specifies in ohms the sensor resistance at 0 deg C. The Callendar-Van Dusen equation requires this value. Refer to the sensor documentation to determine this value.
- [Analog Input:Temperature:RTD:Type](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr1032.html) Specifies the type of RTD connected to the channel.
- [Analog Input:Temperature:Thermistor:A](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr18c9.html) Specifies the 'A' constant of the Steinhart-Hart thermistor equation .
- [Analog Input:Temperature:Thermistor:B](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr18cb.html) Specifies the 'B' constant of the Steinhart-Hart thermistor equation .
- [Analog Input:Temperature:Thermistor:C](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr18ca.html) Specifies the 'C' constant of the Steinhart-Hart thermistor equation .
- [Analog Input:Temperature:Thermistor:R1](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr1061.html) Specifies in ohms the value of the reference resistor for the thermistor if you use voltage excitation. NI-DAQmx ignores this value for current excitation.
- [Analog Input:Temperature:Thermocouple:CJC Channel](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr1034.html) Indicates the channel that acquires the temperature of the cold junction if AI.Thrmcpl.CJCSrc is Channel. If the channel is a temperature channel, NI-DAQmx acquires the temperature in the correct units. Other channel types, such as a resistance channel with a custom sensor, must use a custom scale to scale values to degrees Celsius.
- [Analog Input:Temperature:Thermocouple:CJC Source](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr1035.html) Indicates the source of cold-junction compensation .
- [Analog Input:Temperature:Thermocouple:CJC Value](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr1036.html) Specifies the temperature of the cold junction if AI.Thrmcpl.CJCSrc is Constant Value. Specify this value in the units of the measurement.
- [Analog Input:Temperature:Thermocouple:Scale Type](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr29d0.html) Specifies the method or equation form that the thermocouple scale uses.
- [Analog Input:Temperature:Thermocouple:Type](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr1050.html) Specifies the type of thermocouple connected to the channel. Thermocouple types differ in composition and measurement range.
- [Analog Input:Temperature:Units](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr1033.html) Specifies the units to use to return temperature measurements from the channel.
- [Analog Input:Torque:Units](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr2f77.html) Specifies in which unit to return torque measurements from the channel.
- [Analog Input:Velocity:IEPE Sensor:Sensitivity](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr2ff6.html) Specifies the sensitivity of the IEPE velocity sensor connected to the channel. Specify this value in the unit indicated by AI.Velocity.IEPESensor.SensitivityUnits .
- [Analog Input:Velocity:IEPE Sensor:Sensitivity Units](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr2ff7.html) Specifies the units for AI.Velocity.IEPESensor.Sensitivity .
- [Analog Input:Velocity:IEPE Sensor:dB Reference](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr2ff5.html) Specifies the decibel reference level in the units of the channel. When you read samples as a waveform, the decibel reference level is included in the waveform attributes.
- [Analog Input:Velocity:Units](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr2ff4.html) Specifies in which unit to return velocity measurements from the channel.
- [Analog Input:Voltage:AC RMS Voltage:Units](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr17e2.html) Specifies the units to use to return voltage RMS measurements from the channel.
- [Analog Input:Voltage:Units](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr1094.html) Specifies the units to use to return voltage measurements from the channel.
- [Analog Input:Voltage:dB Reference](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr29b0.html) Specifies the decibel reference level in the units of the channel. When you read samples as a waveform, the decibel reference level is included in the waveform attributes.
- [Analog Output:Current:Units](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr1109.html) Specifies in what units to generate current on the channel. Write data to the channel in the units you select.
- [Analog Output:Custom Scale Name](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr1188.html) Specifies the name of a custom scale for the channel.
- [Analog Output:Function Generation:Amplitude](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr2a1a.html) Specifies the zero-to-peak amplitude of the waveform to generate in volts. Zero and negative values are valid.
- [Analog Output:Function Generation:Frequency](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr2a19.html) Specifies the frequency of the waveform to generate in hertz.
- [Analog Output:Function Generation:Modulation:FM Deviation](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr2a23.html) Specifies the FM deviation in hertz per volt when AO.FuncGen.ModulationType is FM.
- [Analog Output:Function Generation:Modulation:Type](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr2a22.html) Specifies if the device generates a modulated version of the waveform using the original waveform as a carrier and input from an external terminal as the signal.
- [Analog Output:Function Generation:Offset](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr2a1b.html) Specifies the voltage offset of the waveform to generate.
- [Analog Output:Function Generation:Square:DutyCycle](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr2a1c.html) Specifies the square wave duty cycle of the waveform to generate.
- [Analog Output:Function Generation:Start Phase](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr31c4.html) Specifies the starting phase in degrees of the waveform to generate.
- [Analog Output:Function Generation:Type](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr2a18.html) Specifies the kind of the waveform to generate.
- [Analog Output:General Properties:Advanced:Data Transfer and Memory:Data Transfer Mechanism](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr134.html) Specifies the data transfer mode for the device.
- [Analog Output:General Properties:Advanced:Data Transfer and Memory:Data Transfer Request Condition](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr183c.html) Specifies under what condition to transfer data from the buffer to the onboard memory of the device.
- [Analog Output:General Properties:Advanced:Data Transfer and Memory:Memory Mapping for Programmed IO Enable](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr188f.html) Specifies for NI-DAQmx to map hardware registers to the memory space of the application, if possible. Normally, NI-DAQmx maps hardware registers to memory accessible only to the kernel. Mapping the registers to the memory space of the application increases performance. However, if the application accesses the memory space mapped to the registers, it can adversely affect the operation of the device and possibly result in a system crash.
- [Analog Output:General Properties:Advanced:Data Transfer and Memory:USB Transfer Request Count](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr3001.html) Specifies the maximum number of simultaneous USB transfers used to stream data. Modify this value to affect performance under different combinations of operating system and device.
- [Analog Output:General Properties:Advanced:Data Transfer and Memory:USB Transfer Request Size](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr2a8f.html) Specifies the maximum size of a USB transfer request in bytes. Modify this value to affect performance under different combinations of operating system and device.
- [Analog Output:General Properties:Advanced:Data Transfer and Memory:Use Only Onboard Memory](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr183a.html) Specifies whether to write samples directly to the onboard memory of the device, bypassing the memory buffer. Generally, you cannot update onboard memory directly after you start the task. Onboard memory includes data FIFOs.
- [Analog Output:General Properties:Advanced:Device Scaling Coefficients:Device Scaling Coefficients](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr1931.html) Indicates the coefficients of a linear equation that NI-DAQmx uses to scale values from a voltage to the native format of the device. Each element of the array corresponds to a term of the equation. The first element of the array corresponds to the y-intercept, and the second element corresponds to the slope. Scaling coefficients do not account for any custom scales that may be applied to the channel.
- [Analog Output:General Properties:Advanced:Enhanced Image Rejection Enable](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr2241.html) Specifies whether to enable the DAC interpolation filter. Disable the interpolation filter to improve DAC signal-to-noise ratio at the expense of degraded image rejection.
- [Analog Output:General Properties:Advanced:Gain:Gain Value](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr118.html) Specifies in decibels the gain factor to apply to the channel.
- [Analog Output:General Properties:DAC:Offset Voltage:External Source](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr2254.html) Specifies the source of the DAC offset voltage if AO.DAC.Offset.Src is External. The valid sources for this signal vary by device .
- [Analog Output:General Properties:DAC:Offset Voltage:Source](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr2253.html) Specifies the source of the DAC offset voltage. The value of this voltage source determines the full-scale value of the DAC.
- [Analog Output:General Properties:DAC:Offset Voltage:Value](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr2255.html) Specifies in volts the value of the DAC offset voltage. To achieve best accuracy, the DAC offset value should be hand calibrated.
- [Analog Output:General Properties:DAC:Range:High](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr182e.html) Specifies the upper limit of the output range of the device. This value is in the native units of the device. On E Series devices, for example, the native units is volts.
- [Analog Output:General Properties:DAC:Range:Low](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr182d.html) Specifies the lower limit of the output range of the device. This value is in the native units of the device. On E Series devices, for example, the native units is volts.
- [Analog Output:General Properties:DAC:Reference Voltage:Allow Connecting DAC Reference to Ground at Runtime](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr1830.html) Specifies whether to allow grounding the internal DAC reference at run time. You must set this property to TRUE and set AO.DAC.Ref.Src to Internal before you can set AO.DAC.Ref.ConnToGnd to TRUE.
- [Analog Output:General Properties:DAC:Reference Voltage:Connect DAC Reference to Ground](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr130.html) Specifies whether to ground the internal DAC reference. Grounding the internal DAC reference has the effect of grounding all analog output channels and stopping waveform generation across all analog output channels regardless of whether the channels belong to the current task. You can ground the internal DAC reference only when AO.DAC.Ref.Src is Internal and AO.DAC.Ref.AllowConnToGnd is TRUE.
- [Analog Output:General Properties:DAC:Reference Voltage:External Source](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr2252.html) Specifies the source of the DAC reference voltage if AO.DAC.Ref.Src is External. The valid sources for this signal vary by device .
- [Analog Output:General Properties:DAC:Reference Voltage:Source](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr132.html) Specifies the source of the DAC reference voltage. The value of this voltage source determines the full-scale value of the DAC.
- [Analog Output:General Properties:DAC:Reference Voltage:Value](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr1832.html) Specifies in volts the value of the DAC reference voltage. This voltage determines the full-scale range of the DAC. Smaller reference voltages result in smaller ranges, but increased resolution.
- [Analog Output:General Properties:DAC:Reglitching Enable](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr133.html) Specifies whether to enable reglitching. The output of a DAC normally glitches whenever the DAC is updated with a new value. The amount of glitching differs from code to code and is generally largest at major code transitions. Reglitching generates uniform glitch energy at each code transition and provides for more uniform glitches. Uniform glitch energy makes it easier to filter out the noise introduced from glitching during spectrum analysis.
- [Analog Output:General Properties:DAC:Resolution Units](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr182b.html) Specifies the units of AO.Resolution .
- [Analog Output:General Properties:DAC:Resolution Value](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr182c.html) Indicates the resolution of the digital-to-analog converter of the channel. This value is in the units you specify with AO.ResolutionUnits .
- [Analog Output:General Properties:Filter:Filter Delay](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr3075.html) Specifies the amount of time between when the sample is written by the host device and when the sample is output by the DAC. This value is in the units you specify with AO.FilterDelayUnits .
- [Analog Output:General Properties:Filter:Filter Delay Adjustment](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr3072.html) Specifies an additional amount of time to wait between when the sample is written by the host device and when the sample is output by the DAC. This delay adjustment is in addition to the value indicated by AO.FilterDelay . This delay adjustment is in the units you specify with AO.FilterDelayUnits .
- [Analog Output:General Properties:Filter:Filter Delay Units](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr3076.html) Specifies the units of AO.FilterDelay and AO.FilterDelayAdjustment .
- [Analog Output:General Properties:Output Configuration:Common Mode Offset](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr31cc.html) Specifies the common-mode offset of the AO channel. Use the property only when Terminal Configuration is set to Differential.
- [Analog Output:General Properties:Output Configuration:Idle Output Behavior](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr2240.html) Specifies the state of the channel when no generation is in progress.
- [Analog Output:General Properties:Output Configuration:Load Impedance](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr121.html) Specifies in ohms the load impedance connected to the analog output channel.
- [Analog Output:General Properties:Output Configuration:Output Impedance](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr1490.html) Specifies in ohms the impedance of the analog output stage of the device.
- [Analog Output:General Properties:Output Configuration:Terminal Configuration](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr188e.html) Specifies the terminal configuration of the channel.
- [Analog Output:Maximum Value](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr1186.html) Specifies the maximum value you expect to generate. The value is in the units you specify with a units property. If you try to write a value larger than the maximum value, NI-DAQmx generates an error. NI-DAQmx might coerce this value to a smaller value if other task settings restrict the device from generating the desired maximum.
- [Analog Output:Minimum Value](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr1187.html) Specifies the minimum value you expect to generate. The value is in the units you specify with a units property. If you try to write a value smaller than the minimum value, NI-DAQmx generates an error. NI-DAQmx might coerce this value to a larger value if other task settings restrict the device from generating the desired minimum.
- [Analog Output:Output Type](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr1108.html) Indicates whether the channel generates voltage, current, or a waveform.
- [Analog Output:Voltage:Current Limit](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr2a1d.html) Specifies the current limit, in amperes, for the voltage channel.
- [Analog Output:Voltage:Units](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr1184.html) Specifies in what units to generate voltage on the channel. Write data to the channel in the units you select.
- [Counter Input:Count Edges:Active Edge](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr697.html) Specifies on which edges to increment or decrement the counter.
- [Counter Input:Count Edges:Count Direction:Direction](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr696.html) Specifies whether to increment or decrement the counter on each edge.

- [Counter Input:Count Edges:Count Direction:Input:Digital Filter:Timebase:Source](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr21f3.html) Specifies the input terminal of the signal to use as the timebase of the pulse width filter.
- [Counter Input:Count Edges:Count Direction:Input:Digital Synchronization:Enable](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr21f5.html) Specifies whether to synchronize recognition of transitions in the signal to the internal timebase of the device.
- [Counter Input:Count Edges:Count Direction:Input:Hysteresis](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr31b2.html) Specifies a hysteresis level applied to the CI.CountEdges.CountDir.ThreshVoltage . The source signal must fall below CI.CountEdges.CountDir.ThreshVoltage minus the hysteresis before a change in count direction occurs.
- [Counter Input:Count Edges:Count Direction:Input:Logic Level Behavior](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr309e.html) Specifies the logic level behavior on the count reset line.
- [Counter Input:Count Edges:Count Direction:Input:Terminal](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr21e1.html) Specifies the source terminal of the digital signal that controls the count direction if CI.CountEdges.Dir is Externally Controlled.
- [Counter Input:Count Edges:Count Direction:Input:Terminal Configuration](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr309d.html) Specifies the input terminal configuration.
- [Counter Input:Count Edges:Count Direction:Input:Threshold Level](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr31b1.html) Specifies the voltage level applied to the Count Direction terminal. When the signal is above this threshold, the counter counts up. When the signal is below this threshold, the counter counts down.
- [Counter Input:Count Edges:Count Reset:Active Edge](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr2fb2.html) Specifies on which edge of the signal to reset the count.
- [Counter Input:Count Edges:Count Reset:Enable](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr2faf.html) Specifies whether to reset the count on the active edge specified with CI.CountEdges.CountReset.Term .

- [Counter Input:Count Edges:Count Reset:Input:Digital Filter:Timebase:Rate](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr2fb6.html) Specifies in hertz the rate of the pulse width filter timebase. NI-DAQmx uses this value to compute settings for the filter.
- [Counter Input:Count Edges:Count Reset:Input:Digital Filter:Timebase:Source](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr2fb5.html) Specifies the input of the signal to use as the timebase of the pulse width filter.
- [Counter Input:Count Edges:Count Reset:Input:Digital Synchronization:Enable](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr2fb7.html) Specifies whether to synchronize recognition of transitions in the signal to the internal timebase of the device.
- [Counter Input:Count Edges:Count Reset:Input:Hysteresis](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr31b4.html) Specifies a hysteresis level applied to CI.CountEdges.CountReset.ThreshVoltage . When CI.CountEdges.CountReset.ActiveEdge is rising, the source signal must first fall below CI.CountEdges.CountReset.ThreshVoltage minus the hysteresis before a rising edge is detected at CI.CountEdges.CountReset.ThreshVoltage . When CI.CountEdges.CountReset.ActiveEdge is falling, the source signal must first rise above CI.CountEdges.CountReset.ThreshVoltage plus the hysteresis before a falling edge is detected at CI.CountEdges.CountReset.ThreshVoltage .

- [Counter Input:Count Edges:Gate:Input:Digital Filter:Timebase:Source](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr30f3.html) Specifies the input terminal of the signal to use as the timebase of the pulse width filter.
- [Counter Input:Count Edges:Gate:Input:Hysteresis](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr31b6.html) Specifies a hysteresis level applied to the CI.CountEdges.Gate.ThreshVoltage . When CI.CountEdges.Gate.When is High, the source signal must fall below CI.CountEdges.Gate.ThreshVoltage minus the hysteresis before the counter resumes counting. When CI.CountEdges.Gate.When is Low, the source signal must rise above CI.CountEdges.Gate.ThreshVoltage plus the hysteresis before the counter resumes counting.

- [Counter Input:Count Edges:Gate:Input:Terminal Configuration](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr30ef.html) Specifies the gate terminal configuration.
- [Counter Input:Count Edges:Gate:Input:Threshold Level](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr31b5.html) Specifies the voltage level at which to recognize the counter gate signal.
- [Counter Input:Count Edges:Gate:Pause When](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr30f5.html) Specifies whether the counter gates input pulses while the signal is high or low.

- [Counter Input:Count Edges:Input:Threshold Level](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr31af.html) Specifies the voltage level at which to recognize waveform repetitions. Select a voltage level that occurs only once within the entire period of a waveform. You also can select a voltage that occurs only once while the voltage rises or falls.
- [Counter Input:Custom Scale Name](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr189e.html) Specifies the name of a custom scale for the channel.

When CI.Freq.StartingEdge is rising, the source signal must first fall below CI.Freq.ThreshVoltage minus the hysteresis before a rising edge is detected at CI.Freq.ThreshVoltage . When CI.Freq.StartingEdge is falling, the source signal must first rise above CI.Freq.ThreshVoltage plus the hysteresis before a falling edge is detected at CI.Freq.ThreshVoltage .
- [Counter Input:Frequency:Input:Logic Level Behavior](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr3098.html) Specifies the logic level behavior on the input line.
- [Counter Input:Frequency:Input:Terminal](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr18a2.html) Specifies the connectCounter of the signal to measure.
