- [Counter Input:Frequency:Input:Threshold Level](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr31ab.html) Specifies the voltage level at which to recognize waveform repetitions. Select a voltage level that occurs only once within the entire period of a waveform. You also can select a voltage that occurs only once while the voltage rises or falls.
- [Counter Input:Frequency:Measurement Specifications:Enable Averaging](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr2ed0.html) Specifies whether to enable averaging mode for Sample Clock-timed frequency measurements.
- [Counter Input:Frequency:Measurement Specifications:High Frequency:Measurement Time](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr145.html) Specifies in seconds the length of time to measure the frequency of the signal if CI.Freq.MeasMeth is High Frequency with 2 Counters. Measurement accuracy increases with increased measurement time and with increased signal frequency. If you measure a high-frequency signal for too long, however, the count register could roll over, which results in an incorrect measurement.
- [Counter Input:Frequency:Measurement Specifications:Large Range:Divisor](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr147.html) Specifies the value by which to divide the input signal if CI.Freq.MeasMeth is Large Range with 2 Counters. The larger the divisor, the more accurate the measurement. However, too large a value could cause the count register to roll over, which results in an incorrect measurement.
- [Counter Input:Frequency:Measurement Specifications:Method](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr144.html) Specifies the method to use to measure the frequency of the signal.
- [Counter Input:Frequency:Starting Edge](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr799.html) Specifies between which edges to measure the frequency of the signal.
- [Counter Input:Frequency:Units](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr18a1.html) Specifies the units to use to return frequency measurements.
- [Counter Input:General Properties:Counter Timebase:Active Edge](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr142.html) Specifies whether a timebase cycle is from rising edge to rising edge or from falling edge to falling edge.
- [Counter Input:General Properties:Counter Timebase:Digital Filter:Enable](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr2271.html) Specifies whether to apply the pulse width filter to the signal.
- [Counter Input:General Properties:Counter Timebase:Digital Filter:Minimum Pulse Width](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr2272.html) Specifies in seconds the minimum pulse width the filter recognizes.
- [Counter Input:General Properties:Counter Timebase:Digital Filter:Timebase:Rate](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr2274.html) Specifies in hertz the rate of the pulse width filter timebase. NI-DAQmx uses this value to compute settings for the filter.
- [Counter Input:General Properties:Counter Timebase:Digital Filter:Timebase:Source](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr2273.html) Specifies the input terminal of the signal to use as the timebase of the pulse width filter.
- [Counter Input:General Properties:Counter Timebase:Digital Synchronization:Enable](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr2275.html) Specifies whether to synchronize recognition of transitions in the signal to the internal timebase of the device.
- [Counter Input:General Properties:Counter Timebase:Rate](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr18b2.html) Specifies in Hertz the frequency of the counter timebase. Specifying the rate of a counter timebase allows you to take measurements in terms of time or frequency rather than in ticks of the timebase. If you use an external timebase and do not specify the rate, you can take measurements only in terms of ticks of the timebase.
- [Counter Input:General Properties:Counter Timebase:Source](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr143.html) Specifies the terminal of the timebase to use for the counter.
- [Counter Input:General Properties:Filter:Enable](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr31b7.html) Specifies the corresponding filter enable/disable state.
- [Counter Input:General Properties:Filter:Filter Delay](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr31bb.html) Indicates the amount of time between when the input signal transitions and when the filtered sample is read by the host device. This value is in the units specified with CI.FilterDelayUnits .
- [Counter Input:General Properties:Filter:Filter Delay Units](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr31bc.html) Specifies the units of CI.FilterDelay .
- [Counter Input:General Properties:Filter:Frequency](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr31b8.html) Specifies the corresponding filter frequency (cutoff or center) of the filter response.
- [Counter Input:General Properties:Filter:Order](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr31ba.html) Specifies the corresponding filter order and defines the slope of the filter response.
- [Counter Input:General Properties:Filter:Response](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr31b9.html) Specifies the corresponding filter response and defines the shape of the filter response.
- [Counter Input:General Properties:Input Configuration:Voltage Threshold Level](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr30b7.html) Specifies the digital threshold value in Volts for high and low input transitions. Some devices do not support this for differential channels.
- [Counter Input:General Properties:More:Advanced:Data Transfer and Memory:Data Transfer Mechanism](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr200.html) Specifies the data transfer mode for the channel.
- [Counter Input:General Properties:More:Advanced:Data Transfer and Memory:Data Transfer Request Condition](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr2efb.html) Specifies under what condition to transfer data from the onboard memory of the device to the buffer.
- [Counter Input:General Properties:More:Advanced:Data Transfer and Memory:Memory Mapping for Programmed IO Enable](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr2ed2.html) Specifies for NI-DAQmx to map hardware registers to the memory space of the application, if possible. Normally, NI-DAQmx maps hardware registers to memory accessible only to the kernel. Mapping the registers to the memory space of the application increases performance. However, if the application accesses the memory space mapped to the registers, it can adversely affect the operation of the device and possibly result in a system crash.
- [Counter Input:General Properties:More:Advanced:Data Transfer and Memory:Number Of Possibly Invalid Samples](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr193c.html) Indicates the number of samples that the device might have overwritten before it could transfer them to the buffer.
- [Counter Input:General Properties:More:Advanced:Data Transfer and Memory:USB Transfer Request Count](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr3004.html) Specifies the maximum number of simultaneous USB transfers used to stream data. Modify this value to affect performance under different combinations of operating system and device.
- [Counter Input:General Properties:More:Advanced:Data Transfer and Memory:USB Transfer Request Size](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr2a92.html) Specifies the maximum size of a USB transfer request in bytes. Modify this value to affect performance under different combinations of operating system and device.
- [Counter Input:General Properties:More:Advanced:Duplicate Count Prevention](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr21ac.html) Specifies whether to enable duplicate count prevention for the channel. Duplicate count prevention is enabled by default. Setting CI.Prescaler disables duplicate count prevention unless you explicitly enable it.
- [Counter Input:General Properties:More:Advanced:Maximum Measurable Period](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr3095.html) Specifies the maximum period (in seconds) in which the device will recognize signals. For frequency measurements, a signal with a higher period than the one set in this property will return 0 Hz. For duty cycle, the device will return 0 or 1 depending on the state of the line during the max defined period of time. Period measurements will return NaN. Pulse width measurement will return zero.
- [Counter Input:General Properties:More:Advanced:Prescaler](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr2239.html) Specifies the divisor to apply to the signal you connect to the counter source terminal. Scaled data that you read takes this setting into account. You should use a prescaler only when you connect an external signal to the counter source terminal and when that signal has a higher frequency than the fastest onboard timebase. Setting this value disables duplicate count prevention unless you explicitly set CI.DupCountPrevention to TRUE.
- [Counter Input:General Properties:More:Count](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr148.html) Indicates the current value of the count register.
- [Counter Input:General Properties:More:Counter Timebase Master Timebase Divisor](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr18b3.html) Specifies the divisor for an external counter timebase. You can divide the counter timebase in order to measure slower signals without causing the count register to roll over.
- [Counter Input:General Properties:More:Output State](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr149.html) Indicates the current state of the out terminal of the counter.
- [Counter Input:General Properties:More:Sample Clock Overrun Behavior](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr3093.html) Specifies the counter behavior when data is read but a new value was not detected during a sample clock.
- [Counter Input:General Properties:More:Sample Clock Overrun Sentinel Value](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr3094.html) Specifies the sentinel value returned when the No New Sample Behavior is set to Sentinel Value.
- [Counter Input:General Properties:More:Terminal Count Reached](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr150.html) Indicates whether the counter rolled over. When you query this property, NI-DAQmx resets it to FALSE.
- [Counter Input:Maximum Value](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr189c.html) Specifies the maximum value you expect to measure. This value is in the units you specify with a units property. When you query this property, it returns the coerced maximum value that the hardware can measure with the current settings.
- [Counter Input:Measurement Type](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr18a0.html) Indicates the measurement to take with the channel.
- [Counter Input:Minimum Value](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr189d.html) Specifies the minimum value you expect to measure. This value is in the units you specify with a units property. When you query this property, it returns the coerced minimum value that the hardware can measure with the current settings.
- [Counter Input:Period:Input:Digital Filter:Enable](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr21ec.html) Specifies whether to apply the pulse width filter to the signal.
- [Counter Input:Period:Input:Digital Filter:Minimum Pulse Width](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr21ed.html) Specifies in seconds the minimum pulse width the filter recognizes.
- [Counter Input:Period:Input:Digital Filter:Timebase:Rate](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr21ef.html) Specifies in hertz the rate of the pulse width filter timebase. NI-DAQmx uses this value to compute settings for the filter.
- [Counter Input:Period:Input:Digital Filter:Timebase:Source](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr21ee.html) Specifies the input terminal of the signal to use as the timebase of the pulse width filter.
- [Counter Input:Period:Input:Digital Synchronization:Enable](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr21f0.html) Specifies whether to synchronize recognition of transitions in the signal to the internal timebase of the device.
- [Counter Input:Period:Input:Hysteresis](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr31ae.html) Specifies a hysteresis level to apply to CI.Period.ThreshVoltage . When CI.Period.StartingEdge is rising, the source signal must first fall below CI.Period.ThreshVoltage minus the hysteresis before a rising edge is detected at CI.Period.ThreshVoltage . When CI.Period.StartingEdge is falling, the source signal must first rise above CI.Period.ThreshVoltage plus the hysteresis before a falling edge is detected at CI.Period.ThreshVoltage .
- [Counter Input:Period:Input:Logic Level Behavior](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr309a.html) Specifies the logic level behavior on the input line.
- [Counter Input:Period:Input:Terminal](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr18a4.html) Specifies the connectCounter of the signal to measure.
- [Counter Input:Period:Input:Terminal Configuration](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr3099.html) Specifies the input terminal configuration.
- [Counter Input:Period:Input:Threshold Level](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr31ad.html) Specifies the voltage level at which to recognize waveform repetitions. Select a voltage level that occurs only once within the entire period of a waveform. You also can select a voltage that occurs only once while the voltage rises or falls.
- [Counter Input:Period:Measurement Specifications:Enable Averaging](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr2ed1.html) Specifies whether to enable averaging mode for Sample Clock-timed period measurements.
- [Counter Input:Period:Measurement Specifications:High Frequency:Measurement Time](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr192d.html) Specifies in seconds the length of time to measure the period of the signal if CI.Period.MeasMeth is High Frequency with 2 Counters. Measurement accuracy increases with increased measurement time and with increased signal frequency. If you measure a high-frequency signal for too long, however, the count register could roll over, which results in an incorrect measurement.
- [Counter Input:Period:Measurement Specifications:Large Range:Divisor](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr192e.html) Specifies the value by which to divide the input signal if CI.Period.MeasMeth is Large Range with 2 Counters. The larger the divisor, the more accurate the measurement. However, too large a value could cause the count register to roll over, which results in an incorrect measurement.
- [Counter Input:Period:Measurement Specifications:Method](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr192c.html) Specifies the method to use to measure the period of the signal.
- [Counter Input:Period:Starting Edge](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr852.html) Specifies between which edges to measure the period of the signal.
- [Counter Input:Period:Units](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr18a3.html) Specifies the unit to use to return period measurements.

This value is the number of pulses on either signal A or signal B, not the total number of pulses on both signal A and signal B.

X1, X2, and X4 are valid for quadrature encoders only. Two Pulse Counting is valid for two-pulse encoders only.
- [Counter Input:Position:Linear Encoder:Distance Per Pulse](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr911.html) Specifies the distance to measure for each pulse the encoder generates on signal A or signal B. This value is in the units you specify with CI.LinEncoder.Units .

- [Counter Input:Two Edge Separation:Second:Input:Digital Filter:Timebase:Source](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr2216.html) Specifies the input terminal of the signal to use as the timebase of the pulse width filter.
- [Counter Input:Two Edge Separation:Second:Input:Digital Synchronization:Enable](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr2218.html) Specifies whether to synchronize recognition of transitions in the signal to the internal timebase of the device.
- [Counter Input:Two Edge Separation:Second:Input:Logic Level Behavior](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr30ae.html) Specifies the logic level behavior on the count reset line.
- [Counter Input:Two Edge Separation:Second:Input:Terminal](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr18ae.html) Specifies the source terminal of the digital signal that stops each measurement.
- [Counter Input:Two Edge Separation:Second:Input:Terminal Configuration](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr30ad.html) Specifies the input terminal configuration.
- [Counter Input:Two Edge Separation:Units](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr18ac.html) Specifies the units to use to return two-edge separation measurements from the channel.
- [Counter Input:Velocity:A Input:Digital Filter:Enable](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr30e0.html) Specifies whether to apply the pulse width filter to the signal.
- [Counter Input:Velocity:A Input:Digital Filter:Minimum Pulse Width](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr30e1.html) Specifies in seconds the minimum pulse width the digital filter recognizes.
- [Counter Input:Velocity:A Input:Digital Filter:Timebase Rate](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr30e3.html) Specifies in hertz the rate of the pulse width filter timebase. NI-DAQmx uses this value to compute settings for the filter.
- [Counter Input:Velocity:A Input:Digital Filter:Timebase Source](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr30e2.html) Specifies the input terminal of the signal to use as the timebase of the pulse width filter.
- [Counter Input:Velocity:A Input:Logic Level Behavior](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr30df.html) Specifies the logic level behavior of the input terminal.
- [Counter Input:Velocity:A Input:Terminal](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr30dd.html) Specifies the terminal to which signal A is connected.
- [Counter Input:Velocity:A Input:Terminal Configuration](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr30de.html) Specifies the input terminal configuration.
- [Counter Input:Velocity:Advanced:Divisor](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr30ec.html) Specifies the value by which to divide the input signal.
- [Counter Input:Velocity:Advanced:Measurement Time](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr30eb.html) Specifies in seconds the length of time to measure the velocity of the signal.
- [Counter Input:Velocity:Angular Encoder:Pulses Per Revolution](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr30d9.html) Specifies the number of pulses the encoder generates per revolution. This value is the number of pulses on either signal A or signal B, not the total number of pulses on both signal A and signal B.
- [Counter Input:Velocity:Angular Encoder:Units](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr30d8.html) Specifies the units to use to return angular velocity counter measurements.
- [Counter Input:Velocity:B Input:Digital Filter:Enable](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr30e7.html) Specifies whether to apply the pulse width filter to the signal.
- [Counter Input:Velocity:B Input:Digital Filter:Minimum Pulse Width](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr30e8.html) Specifies in seconds the minimum pulse width the digital filter recognizes.
- [Counter Input:Velocity:B Input:Digital Filter:Timebase Rate](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr30ea.html) Specifies in hertz the rate of the pulse width filter timebase. NI-DAQmx uses this value to compute settings for the filter.
- [Counter Input:Velocity:B Input:Digital Filter:Timebase Source](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr30e9.html) Specifies the input terminal of the signal to use as the timebase of the pulse width filter.
- [Counter Input:Velocity:B Input:Logic Level Behavior](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr30e6.html) Specifies the logic level behavior of the input terminal.
- [Counter Input:Velocity:B Input:Terminal](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr30e4.html) Specifies the terminal to which signal B is connected.
- [Counter Input:Velocity:B Input:Terminal Configuration](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr30e5.html) Specifies the input terminal configuration.
- [Counter Input:Velocity:Decoding Type](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr30dc.html) Specifies how to count and interpret the pulses the encoder generates on signal A and signal B. X1, X2, and X4 are valid for quadrature encoders only. Two Pulse Counting is valid for two-pulse encoders only.
- [Counter Input:Velocity:Linear Encoder:Distance per Pulse](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr30db.html) Specifies the distance to measure for each pulse the encoder generates on signal A or signal B. This value is in the units you specify in CI.Velocity.LinEncoder.DistUnits.
- [Counter Input:Velocity:Linear Encoder:Units](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr30da.html) Specifies the units to use to return linear encoder velocity measurements from the channel.
- [Counter Output:General Properties:Counter Timebase:Active Edge](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr341.html) Specifies whether a timebase cycle is from rising edge to rising edge or from falling edge to falling edge.
- [Counter Output:General Properties:Counter Timebase:Digital Filter:Enable](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr2276.html) Specifies whether to apply the pulse width filter to the signal.
- [Counter Output:General Properties:Counter Timebase:Digital Filter:Minimum Pulse Width](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr2277.html) Specifies in seconds the minimum pulse width the filter recognizes.
- [Counter Output:General Properties:Counter Timebase:Digital Filter:Timebase:Rate](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr2279.html) Specifies in hertz the rate of the pulse width filter timebase. NI-DAQmx uses this value to compute settings for the filter.
- [Counter Output:General Properties:Counter Timebase:Digital Filter:Timebase:Source](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr2278.html) Specifies the input terminal of the signal to use as the timebase of the pulse width filter.
- [Counter Output:General Properties:Counter Timebase:Digital Synchronization:Enable](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr227a.html) Specifies whether to synchronize recognition of transitions in the signal to the internal timebase of the device.
- [Counter Output:General Properties:Counter Timebase:Rate](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr18c2.html) Specifies in Hertz the frequency of the counter timebase. Specifying the rate of a counter timebase allows you to define output pulses in seconds rather than in ticks of the timebase. If you use an external timebase and do not specify the rate, you can define output pulses only in ticks of the timebase.
- [Counter Output:General Properties:Counter Timebase:Source](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr339.html) Specifies the terminal of the timebase to use for the counter. Typically, NI-DAQmx uses one of the internal counter timebases when generating pulses. Use this property to specify an external timebase and produce custom pulse widths that are not possible using the internal timebases.
- [Counter Output:General Properties:More:Advanced:Constrained Generation Mode](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr29f2.html) Specifies constraints to apply when the counter generates pulses. Constraining the counter reduces the device resources required for counter operation. Constraining the counter can also allow additional analog or counter tasks on the device to run concurrently. For continuous counter tasks, NI-DAQmx consumes no device resources when the counter is constrained. For finite counter tasks, resource use increases with the frequency regardless of the constraint mode. However, fixed frequency constraints significantly reduce resource usage, and fixed duty cycle constraint marginally reduces it.
- [Counter Output:General Properties:More:Advanced:Data Transfer and Memory:Data Transfer Mechanism](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr2ecc.html) Specifies the data transfer mode for the device. For buffered operations, use DMA or USB Bulk. For non-buffered operations, use Polled.
- [Counter Output:General Properties:More:Advanced:Data Transfer and Memory:Data Transfer Request Condition](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr2ecd.html) Specifies under what condition to transfer data from the buffer to the onboard memory of the device.
- [Counter Output:General Properties:More:Advanced:Data Transfer and Memory:Memory Mapping for Programmed IO Enable](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr2ed3.html) Specifies for NI-DAQmx to map hardware registers to the memory space of the application, if possible. Normally, NI-DAQmx maps hardware registers to memory accessible only to the kernel. Mapping the registers to the memory space of the application increases performance. However, if the application accesses the memory space mapped to the registers, it can adversely affect the operation of the device and possibly result in a system crash.
- [Counter Output:General Properties:More:Advanced:Data Transfer and Memory:USB Transfer Request Count](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr3005.html) Specifies the maximum number of simultaneous USB transfers used to stream data. Modify this value to affect performance under different combinations of operating system and device.
- [Counter Output:General Properties:More:Advanced:Data Transfer and Memory:USB Transfer Request Size](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr2a93.html) Specifies the maximum size of a USB transfer request in bytes. Modify this value to affect performance under different combinations of operating system and device.
- [Counter Output:General Properties:More:Advanced:Data Transfer and Memory:Use Only Onboard Memory](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr2ecb.html) Specifies whether to write samples directly to the onboard memory of the device, bypassing the memory buffer. Generally, you cannot update onboard memory directly after you start the task. Onboard memory includes data FIFOs.
- [Counter Output:General Properties:More:Advanced:Prescaler](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr226d.html) Specifies the divisor to apply to the signal you connect to the counter source terminal. Pulse generations defined by frequency or time take this setting into account, but pulse generations defined by ticks do not. You should use a prescaler only when you connect an external signal to the counter source terminal and when that signal has a higher frequency than the fastest onboard timebase.
- [Counter Output:General Properties:More:Advanced:Ready For New Value](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr22ff.html) Indicates whether the counter is ready for new continuous pulse train values.
- [Counter Output:General Properties:More:Auto Increment Count](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr295.html) Specifies a number of timebase ticks by which to increase the time spent in the idle state for each successive pulse.
- [Counter Output:General Properties:More:Count](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr293.html) Indicates the current value of the count register.
- [Counter Output:General Properties:More:Counter Timebase Master Timebase Divisor](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr18c3.html) Specifies the divisor for an external counter timebase. You can divide the counter timebase in order to generate slower signals without causing the count register to roll over.
- [Counter Output:General Properties:More:Enable Initial Delay on Retrigger](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr2ec9.html) Specifies whether to apply the initial delay to retriggered pulse trains.
- [Counter Output:General Properties:More:Output State](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr294.html) Indicates the current state of the output terminal of the counter.
- [Counter Output:General Properties:More:Pulse Done](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr190e.html) Indicates if the task completed pulse generation. Use this value for retriggerable pulse generation when you need to determine if the device generated the current pulse. For retriggerable tasks, when you query this property, NI-DAQmx resets it to FALSE.
- [Counter Output:Output Type](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr18b5.html) Indicates how to define pulses generated on the channel.
- [Counter Output:Pulse:Frequency:Duty Cycle](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr1176.html) Specifies the duty cycle of the pulses. The duty cycle of a signal is the width of the pulse divided by period. NI-DAQmx uses this ratio and the pulse frequency to determine the width of the pulses and the delay between pulses.
- [Counter Output:Pulse:Frequency:Frequency](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr1178.html) Specifies the frequency of the pulses to generate. This value is in the units you specify with CO.Pulse.Freq.Units or when you create the channel.
- [Counter Output:Pulse:Frequency:Initial Delay](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr299.html) Specifies in seconds the amount of time to wait before generating the first pulse.
- [Counter Output:Pulse:Frequency:Units](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr18d5.html) Specifies the units in which to define pulse frequency.
- [Counter Output:Pulse:Idle State](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr1170.html) Specifies the resting state of the output terminal.
- [Counter Output:Pulse:Output Terminal](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr18e1.html) Specifies on which terminal to generate pulses.
- [Counter Output:Pulse:Ticks:High Ticks](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr1169.html) Specifies the number of ticks the pulse is high.
- [Counter Output:Pulse:Ticks:Initial Delay](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr298.html) Specifies the number of ticks to wait before generating the first pulse.
- [Counter Output:Pulse:Ticks:Low Ticks](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr1171.html) Specifies the number of ticks the pulse is low.
- [Counter Output:Pulse:Time:High Time](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr18ba.html) Specifies the amount of time that the pulse is at a high voltage. This value is in the units you specify with CO.Pulse.Time.Units or when you create the channel.
- [Counter Output:Pulse:Time:Initial Delay](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr18bc.html) Specifies in seconds the amount of time to wait before generating the first pulse.
- [Counter Output:Pulse:Time:Low Time](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr18bb.html) Specifies the amount of time that the pulse is at a low voltage. This value is in the units you specify with CO.Pulse.Time.Units or when you create the channel.
- [Counter Output:Pulse:Time:Units](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr18d6.html) Specifies the units in which to define high and low pulse time.
- [Digital Input:Digital Filter:Enable](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr21d6.html) Specifies whether to enable the digital filter for the line(s) or port(s). You can enable the filter on a line-by-line basis. You do not have to enable the filter for all lines in a channel.
- [Digital Input:Digital Filter:Enable Bus Mode](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr2efe.html) Specifies whether to enable bus mode for digital filtering. If you set this property to TRUE, NI-DAQmx treats all lines that use common filtering settings as a bus. If any line in the bus has jitter, all lines in the bus hold state until the entire bus stabilizes, or until 2 times the minimum pulse width elapses. If you set this property to FALSE, NI-DAQmx filters all lines individually. Jitter in one line does not affect other lines.
- [Digital Input:Digital Filter:Minimum Pulse Width](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr21d7.html) Specifies in seconds the minimum pulse width the filter recognizes as a valid high or low state transition.
- [Digital Input:Digital Filter:Timebase:Rate](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr2ed5.html) Specifies in hertz the rate of the digital filter timebase. NI-DAQmx uses this value to compute settings for the filter.
- [Digital Input:Digital Filter:Timebase:Source](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr2ed4.html) Specifies the terminal of the signal to use as the timebase of the digital filter.
- [Digital Input:Digital Synchronization:Enable](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr2ed6.html) Specifies whether to synchronize recognition of transitions in the signal to the internal timebase of the device.
- [Digital Input:General Properties:Advanced:Acquire On](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr2966.html) Specifies on which edge of the sample clock to acquire samples.
- [Digital Input:General Properties:Advanced:Data Transfer and Memory:Data Transfer Mechanism](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr2263.html) Specifies the data transfer mode for the device.
- [Digital Input:General Properties:Advanced:Data Transfer and Memory:Data Transfer Request Condition](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr2264.html) Specifies under what condition to transfer data from the onboard memory of the device to the buffer.
- [Digital Input:General Properties:Advanced:Data Transfer and Memory:Memory Mapping for Programmed IO Enable](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr296a.html) Specifies for NI-DAQmx to map hardware registers to the memory space of the application, if possible. Normally, NI-DAQmx maps hardware registers to memory accessible only to the kernel. Mapping the registers to the memory space of the application increases performance. However, if the application accesses the memory space mapped to the registers, it can adversely affect the operation of the device and possibly result in a system crash.
- [Digital Input:General Properties:Advanced:Data Transfer and Memory:USB Transfer Request Count](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr3002.html) Specifies the maximum number of simultaneous USB transfers used to stream data. Modify this value to affect performance under different combinations of operating system and device.
- [Digital Input:General Properties:Advanced:Data Transfer and Memory:USB Transfer Request Size](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr2a90.html) Specifies the maximum size of a USB transfer request in bytes. Modify this value to affect performance under different combinations of operating system and device.
- [Digital Input:Invert Lines](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr793.html) Specifies whether to invert the lines in the channel. If you set this property to TRUE, the lines are at high logic when off and at low logic when on.
- [Digital Input:Logic Family](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr296d.html) Specifies the logic family to use for acquisition. A logic family corresponds to voltage thresholds that are compatible with a group of voltage standards. Refer to the device documentation for information on the logic high and logic low voltages for these logic families.
- [Digital Input:Number of Lines](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr2178.html) Indicates the number of digital lines in the channel.
- [Digital Input:Tristate](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr1890.html) Specifies whether to tristate the lines in the channel. If you set this property to TRUE, NI-DAQmx tristates the lines in the channel. If you set this property to FALSE, NI-DAQmx does not modify the configuration of the lines even if the lines were previously tristated. Set this property to FALSE to read lines in other tasks or to read output-only lines.
- [Digital Output:General Properties:Advanced:Data Transfer and Memory:Data Transfer Mechanism](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr2266.html) Specifies the data transfer mode for the device.
- [Digital Output:General Properties:Advanced:Data Transfer and Memory:Data Transfer Request Condition](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr2267.html) Specifies under what condition to transfer data from the buffer to the onboard memory of the device.
- [Digital Output:General Properties:Advanced:Data Transfer and Memory:Memory Mapping for Programmed IO Enable](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr296b.html) Specifies for NI-DAQmx to map hardware registers to the memory space of the application, if possible. Normally, NI-DAQmx maps hardware registers to memory accessible only to the kernel. Mapping the registers to the memory space of the application increases performance. However, if the application accesses the memory space mapped to the registers, it can adversely affect the operation of the device and possibly result in a system crash.
- [Digital Output:General Properties:Advanced:Data Transfer and Memory:USB Transfer Request Count](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr3003.html) Specifies the maximum number of simultaneous USB transfers used to stream data. Modify this value to affect performance under different combinations of operating system and device.
- [Digital Output:General Properties:Advanced:Data Transfer and Memory:USB Transfer Request Size](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr2a91.html) Specifies the maximum size of a USB transfer request in bytes. Modify this value to affect performance under different combinations of operating system and device.
- [Digital Output:General Properties:Advanced:Data Transfer and Memory:Use Only Onboard Memory](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr2265.html) Specifies whether to write samples directly to the onboard memory of the device, bypassing the memory buffer. Generally, you cannot update onboard memory after you start the task. Onboard memory includes data FIFOs.
- [Digital Output:General Properties:Advanced:Generate On](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr2969.html) Specifies on which edge of the sample clock to generate samples.
- [Digital Output:Invert Lines](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr1133.html) Specifies whether to invert the lines in the channel. If you set this property to TRUE, the lines are at high logic when off and at low logic when on.
- [Digital Output:Line States:Done State](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr2968.html) Specifies the state of the lines in a digital output task when the task completes execution .
- [Digital Output:Line States:Paused State](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr2967.html) Specifies the state of the lines in a digital output task when the task pauses.
- [Digital Output:Line States:Start State](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr2972.html) Specifies the state of the lines in a digital output task when the task starts.
- [Digital Output:Logic Family](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr296e.html) Specifies the logic family to use for generation. A logic family corresponds to voltage thresholds that are compatible with a group of voltage standards. Refer to the device documentation for information on the logic high and logic low voltages for these logic families.
- [Digital Output:Number of Lines](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr2179.html) Indicates the number of digital lines in the channel.
- [Digital Output:Output Drive Type](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr1137.html) Specifies the drive type for digital output channels.
- [Digital Output:Overcurrent:Automatic Re-enable](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr2a86.html) Specifies whether to automatically reenable channels after they no longer exceed the current limit specified by DO.Overcurrent.Limit .
- [Digital Output:Overcurrent:Current Limit](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr2a85.html) Specifies the current threshold in Amperes for the channel. A value of 0 means the channel observes no limit. Devices can monitor only a finite number of current thresholds simultaneously. If you attempt to monitor additional thresholds, NI-DAQmx returns an error.
- [Digital Output:Overcurrent:Re-enable Period](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr2a87.html) Specifies the delay in seconds between the time a channel no longer exceeds the current limit and the reactivation of that channel, if DO.Overcurrent.AutoReenable is TRUE.
- [Digital Output:Tristate](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr18f3.html) Specifies whether to stop driving the channel and set it to a high-impedance state. You must commit the task for this setting to take effect.
- [General Properties:Channel Type](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr187f.html) Indicates the type of the virtual channel.
- [General Properties:Description](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr1926.html) Specifies a user-defined description for the channel.
- [General Properties:Is Global](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr2304.html) Indicates whether the channel is a global channel .
- [General Properties:Physical Channel Name](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr18f5.html) Specifies the name of the physical channel upon which this virtual channel is based.
- [General Properties:Synchronization Unlock Behavior](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr313c.html) Specifies the action to take if the target loses its synchronization to the grand master.
- [Power Supply:Current:Advanced:Device Scaling Coefficients](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr31da.html) Indicates the coefficients of the polynomial equation that NI-DAQmx uses to scale values from the native format of the device to amperes. Can be read at any time during a task.
- [Power Supply:Current:Setpoint](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr31d5.html) Specifies the output current, in amperes. If the load draws current greater than the specified value, the device will operate in Constant Current mode.
- [Power Supply:Idle Output Behavior](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr31d8.html) Specifies whether to disable the output or maintain the existing value after the task is uncommitted.
- [Power Supply:Output Enable](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr31d6.html) Specifies whether to enable or disable power module output. Can be set while a task is running. Can be read at any time during a task. When a task is running, the output is enabled immediately. Otherwise, the output is not enabled until the task enters the Committed state.
- [Power Supply:Output State](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr31d7.html) Indicates power channel operating state. Can be read at any time during a task.
- [Power Supply:Remote Sense:Remote Sense](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr31db.html) Specifies whether to use local or remote sense to sense the output voltage. DAQmx Read (Power Supply) will return remote or local voltage based on the Remote Sense attribute value. Reading this property will return the user-defined value.
- [Power Supply:Voltage:Advanced:Device Scaling Coefficients](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr31d9.html) Indicates the coefficients of the polynomial equation that NI-DAQmx uses to scale values from the native format of the device to volts. Can be read at any time during a task.
- [Power Supply:Voltage:Setpoint](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr31d4.html) Specifies the constant output voltage, in volts. Can be set while a task is running. Can be read at any time during a task.

## TOPIC 00566: Analog Input:General Properties:Signal Conditioning:Excitation:AC Excitation:Frequency

- bundle_id: `ni-daqmx-labview-api-ref`
- source_path: `resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr1092.html`

Short Name CI.GPS.SyncMethod Data type ci32.png Permissions Read/Write Resettable True Settable While Task Is Running device-specific Available in Run-Tim

### Counter Input:Timestamp:GPS:Synchronization Method

Specifies the method to use to synchronize the counter to a GPS receiver.

#### Remarks

The following table lists the [characteristics](/csh?productcategories=147794&context=lvcore_lvprop_flags) of this property.

| Short Name | CI.GPS.SyncMethod |
| --- | --- |
| Data type |  |
| Permissions | Read/Write |
| Resettable | True |
| Settable While Task Is Running | device-specific |
| Available in Run-Time Engine | True |

| IRIG-B | 10070 | Use the IRIG-B synchronization method. The GPS receiver sends one synchronization pulse per second, as well as information about the number of days, hours, minutes, and seconds that elapsed since the beginning of the current year. |
| --- | --- | --- |
| PPS | 10080 | Use the PPS synchronization method. The GPS receiver sends one synchronization pulse per second, but does not send any timing information. The timestamp measurement returns the number of seconds that elapsed since the device powered up unless you set CI.Timestamp.InitialSeconds . |
| None | 10230 | Do not synchronize the counter to a GPS receiver. The timestamp measurement returns the number of seconds that elapsed since the device powered up unless you set CI.Timestamp.InitialSeconds . |

- source_path: `resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr1176.html`

- source_description: Specifies the duty cycle of the pulses. The duty cycle of a signal is the width of the pulse divided by period. NI-DAQmx uses this ratio and the pulse frequency to determine the width of the pulses and the delay between pulses. Remarks The following table lists the characteristics of this property.

### Counter Output:Pulse:Frequency:Duty Cycle

Specifies the duty cycle of the pulses. The duty cycle of a signal is the width of the pulse divided by period. NI-DAQmx uses this ratio and the pulse frequency to determine the width of the pulses and the delay between pulses.

#### Remarks

The following table lists the [characteristics](/csh?productcategories=147794&context=lvcore_lvprop_flags) of this property.

| --- | --- |

| Resettable | True |
| Settable While Task Is Running | device-specific |
| Available in Run-Time Engine | True |

## TOPIC 00595: Analog Output:Maximum Value

- bundle_id: `ni-daqmx-labview-api-ref`
- source_path: `resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr1186.html`
- source_url: https://docs-be.ni.com/bundle/ni-daqmx-labview-api-ref/raw/resource/enus/resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr1186.html
- document_id: `ni-daqmx-labview-api-ref`
- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: `reference`
- source_description: Specifies the maximum value you expect to generate. The value is in the units you specify with a units property. If you try to write a value larger than the maximum value, NI-DAQmx generates an error. NI-DAQmx might coerce this value to a smaller value if other task settings restrict the device from

### Analog Output:Maximum Value

Specifies the maximum value you expect to generate. The value is in the units you specify with a units property. If you try to write a value larger than the maximum value, NI-DAQmx generates an error. NI-DAQmx might coerce this value to a smaller value if other task settings restrict the device from generating the desired maximum.

#### Remarks

The following table lists the [characteristics](/csh?productcategories=147794&context=lvcore_lvprop_flags) of this property.

| Short Name | AO.Max |
| --- | --- |
| Data type |  |
| Permissions | Read/Write |
| Resettable | True |
| Settable While Task Is Running | device-specific |
| Available in Run-Time Engine | True |

Parent topic:

- content_type: `reference`

Grounding the internal DAC reference has the effect of grounding all analog output channels and stopping waveform generation across all analog output channels regardless of whether the channels belong to the current task. You can ground the int

### Analog Output:General Properties:DAC:Reference Voltage:Connect DAC Reference to Ground

Specifies whether to ground the internal DAC reference. Grounding the internal DAC reference has the effect of grounding all analog output channels and stopping waveform generation across all analog output channels regardless of whether the channels belong to the current task. You can ground the internal DAC reference only when 
 [AO.DAC.Ref.Src](/csh?context=nidaqmx_daqmxprop_attr132)
 is Internal and 
 [AO.DAC.Ref.AllowConnToGnd](/csh?context=nidaqmx_daqmxprop_attr1830)
 is TRUE.

| --- | --- |
| Data type |  |
| Permissions | Read/Write |
| Resettable | True |
| Settable While Task Is Running | device-specific |
| Available in Run-Time Engine | True |

## TOPIC 00601: Analog Output:General Properties:DAC:Reglitching Enable

- bundle_id: `ni-daqmx-labview-api-ref`
- source_path: `resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr133.html`
- source_url: https://docs-be.ni.com/bundle/ni-daqmx-labview-api-ref/raw/resource/enus/resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr133.html
- document_id: `ni-daqmx-labview-api-ref`
- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: `reference`
- source_description: Specifies whether to enable reglitching. The output of a DAC normally glitches whenever the DAC is updated with a new value. The amount of glitching differs from code to code and is generally largest at major code transitions. Reglitching generates uniform glitch energy at each code transition and p

### Analog Output:General Properties:DAC:Reglitching Enable

Specifies whether to enable reglitching. The output of a DAC normally glitches whenever the DAC is updated with a new value. The amount of glitching differs from code to code and is generally largest at major code transitions. Reglitching generates uniform glitch energy at each code transition and provides for more uniform glitches. Uniform glitch energy makes it easier to filter out the noise introduced from glitching during spectrum analysis.

#### Remarks

The following table lists the [characteristics](/csh?productcategories=147794&context=lvcore_lvprop_flags) of this property.

| Short Name | AO.ReglitchEnable |
| --- | --- |
| Data type |  |
| Permissions | Read/Write |
| Resettable | True |
| Settable While Task Is Running | device-specific |
| Available in Run-Time Engine | True |

Parent topic:

DAQmx Channel Properties

## TOPIC 00604: Counter Input:General Properties:Counter Timebase:Source

- bundle_id: `ni-daqmx-labview-api-ref`
- source_path: `resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr143.html`
- source_url: https://docs-be.ni.com/bundle/ni-daqmx-labview-api-ref/raw/resource/enus/resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr143.html
- document_id: `ni-daqmx-labview-api-ref`
- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: `reference`
- source_description: Specifies the terminal of the timebase to use for the counter. Typically, NI-DAQmx uses one of the internal counter timebases when performing counter measurements. Use this property to specify an external timebase and produce custom measurement ranges that are not possible with the internal timebase

### Counter Input:General Properties:Counter Timebase:Source

Specifies the 
 [terminal](/csh?context=nidaqmx_mxcncpts_terminal)
 of the timebase to use for the counter.

Typically, NI-DAQmx uses one of the internal counter timebases when performing counter measurements. Use this property to specify an external 
timebase and produce custom measurement ranges that are not possible with the internal timebases.

You also can use this property to chain counters together. By using the output of a counter as the timebase of another counter, you can effectively 
widen a counter. For example, you can chain two 24 bit counters together to produce one 48 bit counter.

#### Remarks

The following table lists the [characteristics](/csh?productcategories=147794&context=lvcore_lvprop_flags) of this property.

| Short Name | CI.CtrTimebaseSrc |
| --- | --- |
| Data type |  |
| Permissions | Read/Write |
| Resettable | True |
| Settable While Task Is Running | device-specific |
| Available in Run-Time Engine | True |

Parent topic:

DAQmx Channel Properties

| Low Frequency with 1 Counter | 10105 | Use one counter that uses a constant timebase to measure the input signal. |

| Large Range with 2 Counters | 10205 | Use one counter to divide the frequency of the input signal to create a lower-frequency signal that the second counter can more easily measure. |
| Dynamic Averaging | 16065 | Uses one counter with configuration options to control the amount of averaging or filtering applied to the counter measurements. Set filtering options to balance measurement accuracy and noise versus latency. |

| --- | --- | --- |
| Once | 10244 | Perform an auto zero at the beginning of the acquisition. This auto zero task might not run if you have used DAQmx Control Task previously in your task. |
| Every Sample | 10164 | Perform an auto zero at every sample of the acquisition. |

## TOPIC 00623: Analog Input:General Properties:Signal Conditioning:Bridge:Initial Bridge Voltage

- bundle_id: `ni-daqmx-labview-api-ref`
- source_path: `resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr17ed.html`
- source_url: https://docs-be.ni.com/bundle/ni-daqmx-labview-api-ref/raw/resource/enus/resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr17ed.html
- document_id: `ni-daqmx-labview-api-ref`
- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: `reference`
- source_description: Specifies in volts the output voltage of the bridge while not under load. NI-DAQmx subtracts this value from any measurements before applying scaling equations. If you set AI.Bridge.InitialRatio , NI-DAQmx coerces this property to AI.Bridge.InitialRatio times AI.Excit.ActualVal . This property is se

### Analog Input:General Properties:Signal Conditioning:Bridge:Initial Bridge Voltage

Specifies in volts the output voltage of the bridge while not under load. NI-DAQmx subtracts this value from any measurements before applying scaling equations. If you set 
 [AI.Bridge.InitialRatio](/csh?context=nidaqmx_daqmxprop_attr2f86)
 , NI-DAQmx coerces this property to 
 [AI.Bridge.InitialRatio](/csh?context=nidaqmx_daqmxprop_attr2f86)
 times 
 [AI.Excit.ActualVal](/csh?context=nidaqmx_daqmxprop_attr1883)
 . This property is set by DAQmx Perform Bridge Offset Nulling Calibration. If you set this property, NI-DAQmx coerces 
 [AI.Bridge.InitialRatio](/csh?context=nidaqmx_daqmxprop_attr2f86)
 to the value of this property divided by 
 [AI.Excit.ActualVal](/csh?context=nidaqmx_daqmxprop_attr1883)
 . If you set both this property and 
 [AI.Bridge.InitialRatio](/csh?context=nidaqmx_daqmxprop_attr2f86)
 , and their values conflict, NI-DAQmx returns an error. To avoid this error, reset one property to its default value before setting the other.

#### Remarks

The following table lists the [characteristics](/csh?productcategories=147794&context=lvcore_lvprop_flags) of this property.

| Short Name | AI.Bridge.InitialVoltage |
| --- | --- |
| Data type |  |
| Permissions | Read/Write |
| Resettable | True |
| Settable While Task Is Running | device-specific |
| Available in Run-Time Engine | True |

Parent topic:

DAQmx Channel Properties

## TOPIC 00632: Analog Input:General Properties:Signal Conditioning:Excitation:Advanced:Use Excitation For Scaling

- bundle_id: `ni-daqmx-labview-api-ref`
- source_path: `resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr17fc.html`
- source_url: https://docs-be.ni.com/bundle/ni-daqmx-labview-api-ref/raw/resource/enus/resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr17fc.html
- document_id: `ni-daqmx-labview-api-ref`
- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: `reference`
- source_description: Specifies if NI-DAQmx divides the measurement by the excitation. You should typically set this property to TRUE for ratiometric transducers. If you set this property to TRUE, set AI.Max and AI.Min to reflect the scaling. For example, if you expect to acquire a voltage between -5 and 5, and you use a

### Analog Input:General Properties:Signal Conditioning:Excitation:Advanced:Use Excitation For Scaling

Specifies if NI-DAQmx divides the measurement by the excitation. You should typically set this property to TRUE for ratiometric transducers. If you set this property to TRUE, set 
 [AI.Max](/csh?context=nidaqmx_daqmxprop_attr17dd)
 and 
 [AI.Min](/csh?context=nidaqmx_daqmxprop_attr17de)
 to reflect the scaling.

For example, if you expect to acquire a voltage between -5 and 5, and you use an excitation of .10 volts to scale
the measurement, set 
 [AI.Min](/csh?context=nidaqmx_daqmxprop_attr17de)
 to -50 and set 
 [AI.Max](/csh?context=nidaqmx_daqmxprop_attr17dd)
 to 50. If you set 
 [AI.Bridge.Cfg](/csh?context=nidaqmx_daqmxprop_attr87)
 to No Bridge, this 
property has no effect on the measurement.

#### Remarks

The following table lists the [characteristics](/csh?productcategories=147794&context=lvcore_lvprop_flags) of this property.

| Short Name | AI.Excit.UseForScaling |
| --- | --- |
| Data type |  |
| Permissions | Read/Write |
| Resettable | True |
| Settable While Task Is Running | device-specific |
| Available in Run-Time Engine | True |

Parent topic:

### Analog Input:General Properties:Signal Conditioning:Excitation:Advanced:Actual Excitation Value

Specifies the actual amount of excitation supplied by an internal excitation source. If you read an internal excitation source more precisely with an external device, set this property to the value you read. NI-DAQmx ignores this value for external excitation. When performing shunt calibration, some devices set this property automatically.

### Analog Input:General Properties:Filter:Analog Filter:Lowpass:Advanced:Switched Capacitor:External Clock Frequency

- content_type: `reference`
- source_description: Specifies for NI-DAQmx to map hardware registers to the memory space of the application, if possible. Normally, NI-DAQmx maps hardware registers to memory accessible only to the kernel. Mapping the registers to the memory space of the application increases performance. However, if the application ac

### Analog Input:General Properties:Advanced:Data Transfer and Memory:Memory Mapping for Programmed IO Enable

Specifies for NI-DAQmx to map hardware registers to the memory space of the application, if possible. Normally, NI-DAQmx maps hardware registers to memory accessible only to the kernel. Mapping the registers to the memory space of the application increases performance. However, if the application accesses the memory space mapped to the registers, it can adversely affect the operation of the device and possibly result in a system crash.

#### Remarks

The following table lists the [characteristics](/csh?productcategories=147794&context=lvcore_lvprop_flags) of this property.

| Short Name | AI.MemMapEnable |
| --- | --- |
| Data type |  |
| Permissions | Read/Write |
| Resettable | True |
| Settable While Task Is Running | device-specific |
| Available in Run-Time Engine | True |

Parent topic:

- source_url: https://docs-be.ni.com/bundle/ni-daqmx-labview-api-ref/raw/resource/enus/resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr188f.html
- document_id: `ni-daqmx-labview-api-ref`
- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: `reference`
- source_description: Specifies for NI-DAQmx to map hardware registers to the memory space of the application, if possible. Normally, NI-DAQmx maps hardware registers to memory accessible only to the kernel. Mapping the registers to the memory space of the application increases performance. However, if the application ac

### Analog Output:General Properties:Advanced:Data Transfer and Memory:Memory Mapping for Programmed IO Enable

Specifies for NI-DAQmx to map hardware registers to the memory space of the application, if possible. Normally, NI-DAQmx maps hardware registers to memory accessible only to the kernel. Mapping the registers to the memory space of the application increases performance. However, if the application accesses the memory space mapped to the registers, it can adversely affect the operation of the device and possibly result in a system crash.

#### Remarks

The following table lists the [characteristics](/csh?productcategories=147794&context=lvcore_lvprop_flags) of this property.

| Short Name | AO.MemMapEnable |
| --- | --- |
| Data type |  |
| Permissions | Read/Write |
| Resettable | True |
| Settable While Task Is Running | device-specific |
| Available in Run-Time Engine | True |

Parent topic:

DAQmx Channel Properties

## TOPIC 00660: Digital Input:Tristate

- bundle_id: `ni-daqmx-labview-api-ref`
- source_path: `resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr1890.html`
- source_url: https://docs-be.ni.com/bundle/ni-daqmx-labview-api-ref/raw/resource/enus/resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr1890.html
- document_id: `ni-daqmx-labview-api-ref`
- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: `reference`
- source_description: Specifies whether to tristate the lines in the channel. If you set this property to TRUE, NI-DAQmx tristates the lines in the channel. If you set this property to FALSE, NI-DAQmx does not modify the configuration of the lines even if the lines were previously tristated. Set this property to FALSE to

### Digital Input:Tristate

Specifies whether to tristate the lines in the channel. If you set this property to TRUE, NI-DAQmx tristates the lines in the channel. If you set this property to FALSE, NI-DAQmx does not modify the configuration of the lines even if the lines were previously tristated. Set this property to FALSE to read lines in other tasks or to read output-only lines.

#### Remarks

The following table lists the [characteristics](/csh?productcategories=147794&context=lvcore_lvprop_flags) of this property.

| Short Name | DI.Tristate |
| --- | --- |
| Data type |  |
| Permissions | Read/Write |
| Resettable | True |
| Settable While Task Is Running | device-specific |
| Available in Run-Time Engine | True |

Parent topic:

| Velocity:Angular Encoder | 16078 | Angular velocity measurement using an angular encoder. |
| Velocity:Linear Encoder | 16079 | Linear velocity measurement using a linear encoder. |
| Two Edge Separation | 10267 | Measure time between edges of two digital signals. |
| GPS Timestamp | 10362 | Timestamp measurement, synchronizing the counter to a GPS receiver. |

## TOPIC 00677: Counter Input:General Properties:Counter Timebase:Rate

- bundle_id: `ni-daqmx-labview-api-ref`
- source_path: `resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr18b2.html`
- source_url: https://docs-be.ni.com/bundle/ni-daqmx-labview-api-ref/raw/resource/enus/resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr18b2.html
- document_id: `ni-daqmx-labview-api-ref`
- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: `reference`
- source_description: Specifies in Hertz the frequency of the counter timebase. Specifying the rate of a counter timebase allows you to take measurements in terms of time or frequency rather than in ticks of the timebase. If you use an external timebase and do not specify the rate, you can take measurements only in terms

### Counter Input:General Properties:Counter Timebase:Rate

Specifies in Hertz the frequency of the counter timebase. Specifying the rate of a counter timebase allows you to take measurements in terms of time or frequency rather than in ticks of the timebase. If you use an external timebase and do not specify the rate, you can take measurements only in terms of ticks of the timebase.

#### Remarks

The following table lists the [characteristics](/csh?productcategories=147794&context=lvcore_lvprop_flags) of this property.

| Short Name | CI.CtrTimebaseRate |
| --- | --- |
| Data type |  |
| Permissions | Read/Write |
| Resettable | True |
| Settable While Task Is Running | device-specific |
| Available in Run-Time Engine | True |

Parent topic:

DAQmx Channel Properties

## TOPIC 00693: Digital Output:Tristate

- bundle_id: `ni-daqmx-labview-api-ref`
- source_path: `resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr18f3.html`
- source_url: https://docs-be.ni.com/bundle/ni-daqmx-labview-api-ref/raw/resource/enus/resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr18f3.html
- document_id: `ni-daqmx-labview-api-ref`
- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: `reference`
- source_description: Specifies whether to stop driving the channel and set it to a high-impedance state. You must commit the task for this setting to take effect. Setting this property before you commit the task determines whether NI-DAQmx drives data on the channel or tristates the channel after the task transitions to

### Digital Output:Tristate

Specifies whether to stop driving the channel and set it to a high-impedance state. You must commit the task for this setting to take effect.

Setting this property before you 
 [commit](/csh?context=nidaqmx_mxcncpts_committed)
 the task determines whether NI-DAQmx drives data on the channel or tristates the channel after the task 
transitions to the committed state.

Use this property when you want to read and write to channels in a task. Set this property to TRUE before you read from the channel 
and set this property to FALSE before you write to the channel.

When you read from an output channel that is not tristated, the value corresponds to the current value you are driving on the channel.

When you write to a channel that is tristated, no change occurs until you set this property to FALSE. After you set this property to FALSE, 
the value NI-DAQmx drives on the channel corresponds to the last value written to the channel.

Ensure the channel is tristated before any external devices that you connect to the channel drive data onto the channel. Failure to do so could 
result in double-driving the channel and damaging the device.

This property is supported only for line-configurable, bidirectional ports.

#### Remarks

The following table lists the [characteristics](/csh?productcategories=147794&context=lvcore_lvprop_flags) of this property.

| Short Name | DO.Tristate |
| --- | --- |
| Data type |  |
| Permissions | Read/Write |
| Resettable | True |
| Settable While Task Is Running | device-specific |
| Available in Run-Time Engine | True |

Parent topic:

DAQmx Channel Properties

## TOPIC 00704: Counter Input:General Properties:More:Advanced:Data Transfer and Memory:Number Of Possibly Invalid Samples

- bundle_id: `ni-daqmx-labview-api-ref`
- source_path: `resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr193c.html`
- source_url: https://docs-be.ni.com/bundle/ni-daqmx-labview-api-ref/raw/resource/enus/resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr193c.html
- document_id: `ni-daqmx-labview-api-ref`
- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: `reference`
- source_description: Indicates the number of samples that the device might have overwritten before it could transfer them to the buffer. On certain devices during finite buffered time measurements, it is not possible to detect if the counter overwrites a value it read before the device could transfer the sample to the b

### Counter Input:General Properties:More:Advanced:Data Transfer and Memory:Number Of Possibly Invalid Samples

Indicates the number of samples that the device might have overwritten before it could transfer them to the buffer.

On certain devices during finite buffered time measurements, it is not possible to detect if the counter overwrites a value it read before 
the device could transfer the sample to the buffer. This uncertainty is present only when 
 [CI.DataXferMech](/csh?context=nidaqmx_daqmxprop_attr200)
 is DMA and occurs as the acquisition nears 
completion.

Once the acquisition completes, it is impossible to tell if the status value on the counter indicates an overwrite as a result of a true overwrite, 
or because the counter detected another edge of the input signal after the acquisition completed but before the counter could disarm. As a result of this behavior, 
higher frequency input signals are more likely to increase the number of possibly invalid samples.

To decrease the number of possibly invalid samples, read more often from the buffer. Reading from the buffer forces a check on the hardware status and ensures all data is 
valid up to the present point in the buffer. By default, NI-DAQmx checks the validity of data every fourth of the buffer. If you do not perform a read 
until after the device acquires all data, the value of this property is one-fourth of the buffer size or zero.

The value this property indicates is valid only while the task is in the running state. The value of this property while the task is in any other 
state is zero.

#### Remarks

The following table lists the [characteristics](/csh?productcategories=147794&context=lvcore_lvprop_flags) of this property.

| Short Name | CI.NumPossiblyInvalidSamps |
| --- | --- |
| Data type |  |
| Permissions | Read Only |
| Resettable | False |
| Settable While Task Is Running | device-specific |
| Available in Run-Time Engine | True |

Parent topic:

DAQmx Channel Properties

<!--NI_TOPIC bundle=ni-daqmx-labview-api-ref path=resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr193f.html language=enus -->

## TOPIC 00706: Counter Input:General Properties:More:Advanced:Data Transfer and Memory:Data Transfer Mechanism

- bundle_id: `ni-daqmx-labview-api-ref`
- source_path: `resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr200.html`
- source_url: https://docs-be.ni.com/bundle/ni-daqmx-labview-api-ref/raw/resource/enus/resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr200.html
- document_id: `ni-daqmx-labview-api-ref`
- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: `reference`
- source_description: Specifies the data transfer mode for the channel. Remarks The following table lists the characteristics of this property. Short Name CI.DataXferMech Data type ci32.png Permissions Read/Write Resettable True Settable While Task Is Running device-specific Available in Run-Time Engine True DMA 10054 Di

### Counter Input:General Properties:More:Advanced:Data Transfer and Memory:Data Transfer Mechanism

Specifies the data transfer mode for the channel.

#### Remarks

The following table lists the [characteristics](/csh?productcategories=147794&context=lvcore_lvprop_flags) of this property.

| Short Name | CI.DataXferMech |
| --- | --- |
| Data type |  |
| Permissions | Read/Write |
| Resettable | True |
| Settable While Task Is Running | device-specific |
| Available in Run-Time Engine | True |

| DMA | 10054 | Direct Memory Access. Data transfers take place independently from the application. |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Interrupts | 10204 | Data transfers take place independently from the application. Using interrupts increases CPU usage because the CPU must service interrupt requests. Typically, you should use interrupts if the device is out of DMA channels. |
| Programmed I/O | 10264 | Data transfers take place when you call DAQmx Read or DAQmx Write . |
| USB Bulk | 12590 | Data transfers take place independently from the application using a USB bulk pipe. |

Parent topic:

### Analog Input:General Properties:Input Configuration:Input Source

- source_description: Specifies the source terminal of the digital signal that controls the count direction if CI.CountEdges.Dir is Externally Controlled. Remarks The following table lists the characteristics of this property. Short Name CI.CountEdges.DirTerm Data type cdaqmxscale.png Permissions Read/Write Resettable Tr

### Counter Input:Count Edges:Count Direction:Input:Terminal

Specifies the source 
 [terminal](/csh?context=nidaqmx_mxcncpts_terminal)
 of the digital signal that controls the count direction if 
 [CI.CountEdges.Dir](/csh?context=nidaqmx_daqmxprop_attr696)
 is Externally Controlled.

## TOPIC 00723: Counter Input:Position:Decoding Type

- bundle_id: `ni-daqmx-labview-api-ref`
- source_path: `resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr21e6.html`
- source_url: https://docs-be.ni.com/bundle/ni-daqmx-labview-api-ref/raw/resource/enus/resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr21e6.html
- document_id: `ni-daqmx-labview-api-ref`
- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: `reference`
- source_description: Specifies how to count and interpret the pulses the encoder generates on signal A and signal B. X1, X2, and X4 are valid for quadrature encoders only. Two Pulse Counting is valid for two-pulse encoders only. X2 and X4 decoding are more sensitive to smaller changes in position than X1 encoding, with

### Counter Input:Position:Decoding Type

Specifies how to count and interpret the pulses the encoder generates on signal A and signal B. X1, X2, and X4 are valid for 
 [quadrature encoders](/csh?context=nidaqmx_measfunds_quadencoders)
 only. Two Pulse Counting is valid for 
 [two-pulse encoders](/csh?context=nidaqmx_measfunds_twopulse)
 only.

X2 and X4 decoding are more sensitive to smaller changes in position than X1 encoding, with X4 being the most sensitive. However, more sensitive decoding is more likely to produce erroneous measurements if vibration exists in the encoder or other noise exists in the signals.

#### Remarks

The following table lists the [characteristics](/csh?productcategories=147794&context=lvcore_lvprop_flags) of this property.

| Short Name | CI.Encoder.DecodingType |
| --- | --- |
| Data type |  |
| Permissions | Read/Write |
| Resettable | True |
| Settable While Task Is Running | device-specific |
| Available in Run-Time Engine | True |

| X1 | 10090 | If signal A leads signal B, count the rising edges of signal A. If signal B leads signal A, count the falling edges of signal A. |
| --- | --- | --- |
| X2 | 10091 | Count the rising and falling edges of signal A. |
| X4 | 10092 | Count the rising and falling edges of signal A and signal B. |
| Two Pulse Counting | 10313 | Increment the count on rising edges of signal A. Decrement the count on rising edges of signal B. |

Parent topic:

DAQmx Channel Properties

## TOPIC 00728: Counter Input:Frequency:Input:Digital Synchronization:Enable

- bundle_id: `ni-daqmx-labview-api-ref`
- source_path: `resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr21eb.html`
- source_url: https://docs-be.ni.com/bundle/ni-daqmx-labview-api-ref/raw/resource/enus/resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr21eb.html
- document_id: `ni-daqmx-labview-api-ref`
- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: `reference`
- source_description: Specifies whether to synchronize recognition of transitions in the signal to the internal timebase of the device. This property does not affect the minimum pulse width recognized by the device, but setting this property to TRUE does limit the speed at which the device recognizes transitions to less

### Counter Input:Frequency:Input:Digital Synchronization:Enable

Specifies whether to synchronize recognition of transitions in the signal to the internal timebase of the device.

This property does not affect the minimum pulse width recognized by the device, 
but setting this property to TRUE does limit the speed at which the device recognizes transitions 
to less than the frequency of the internal timebase.

#### Remarks

The following table lists the [characteristics](/csh?productcategories=147794&context=lvcore_lvprop_flags) of this property.

| Short Name | CI.Freq.DigSync.Enable |
| --- | --- |
| Data type |  |
| Permissions | Read/Write |
| Resettable | True |
| Settable While Task Is Running | device-specific |
| Available in Run-Time Engine | True |

Parent topic:

DAQmx Channel Properties

<!--NI_TOPIC bundle=ni-daqmx-labview-api-ref path=resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr21f5.html language=enus -->
## TOPIC 00738: Counter Input:Count Edges:Count Direction:Input:Digital Synchronization:Enable

- bundle_id: `ni-daqmx-labview-api-ref`
- source_path: `resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr21f5.html`
- source_url: https://docs-be.ni.com/bundle/ni-daqmx-labview-api-ref/raw/resource/enus/resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr21f5.html
- document_id: `ni-daqmx-labview-api-ref`
- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: `reference`
- source_description: Specifies whether to synchronize recognition of transitions in the signal to the internal timebase of the device. This property does not affect the minimum pulse width recognized by the device, but setting this property to TRUE does limit the speed at which the device recognizes transitions to less

### Counter Input:Count Edges:Count Direction:Input:Digital Synchronization:Enable

Specifies whether to synchronize recognition of transitions in the signal to the internal timebase of the device.

This property does not affect the minimum pulse width recognized by the device, 
but setting this property to TRUE does limit the speed at which the device recognizes transitions 
to less than the frequency of the internal timebase.

#### Remarks

The following table lists the [characteristics](/csh?productcategories=147794&context=lvcore_lvprop_flags) of this property.

| Short Name | CI.CountEdges.CountDir.DigSync.Enable |
| --- | --- |
| Data type |  |
| Permissions | Read/Write |
| Resettable | True |
| Settable While Task Is Running | device-specific |
| Available in Run-Time Engine | True |

Parent topic:

DAQmx Channel Properties
